Public Telegram

To the Shen Bao newspaper, from Kaifeng: Recently, we read in your newspaper about the Yellow River breaking through the Guantai levee. This is not in accordance with the facts. The Guantai closure dam has already accumulated six to seven hundred meters of dry beach towards the river. It is still two to three li away from the main current, and the water has not yet flooded the beach. How could there be a breach? A couple of collapses occurred recently due to the sandy soil, which is inevitable given the years of decay in the willow dikes of the Yellow River embankment. We have ordered the River Bureau and the Fengqiu County government to immediately mobilize laborers to reinforce the earthworks and complete the repairs. There is no dangerous engineering to be addressed. Furthermore, the Guantai closure project was completed in April of the 24th year of the Republic and was inspected and accepted by officials dispatched by the National Government. It was then handed over to the Henan River Bureau for reception and management. This was reported long ago. Years have passed, and the Henan River Bureau is fully responsible for the repairs and maintenance. As the safety of the dikes is concerned, please check and correct your report to clarify the true situation. This is our earnest hope. Yellow River Conservancy Commission, East.

Travel Journal of Japan (11)

— Shen Bao Reporter Hu Zhongchi and Hu Yizang

In the reception room of the Editorial Bureau, we met with Mr. Kamio Shigeru, head of the East Asia Department, reporter Hongo Gaichi of the Communications Department, and pilot Shinno. Mr. Kamio and Mr. Shinno met when the Asahi visiting aircraft arrived in Shanghai last year. Mr. Hongo is a reporter stationed in Beiping who recently returned to Japan. With the guidance of these three friendly colleagues, we gained a general understanding of the internal organization of the Asahi Shimbun. (Note) In the middle of the conversation, Mr. Kamio asked us a question: "Why do your people always look forward to the Sino-Japanese and Russo-Japanese Wars?" "How strange! Where did you hear that? We believe that at least the general intellectuals in our country definitely do not want our two neighboring countries to go to war. Because everyone knows that once a war breaks out, we will become the second Belgium." This was our reply.

We talked with the three Asahi reporters for half an hour. Then, an Asahi employee responsible for "annai" (guided tours) accompanied us to visit various departments within the company. The Asahi Shimbun is a cultural institution that Japan can be proud of. Any group that visits Osaka must visit it. Therefore, there are visitors every day, especially during the so-called tourist season between spring and summer. We followed a tourist group from the countryside and a group of elementary school students, following the designated tour route step by step, passing through many corridors with iron railings along the walls. These corridors are half-wall high and are specially designed for visitors. Each department also has wooden signs hanging high, with simple explanations, also specially for visitors. First, we saw the photo telegraph machine in the photo telegraph room. This is said to be the world's most sophisticated Si Du Jia Luo Lusi·Tai Leifen Gen-style machine, connected to ordinary telephone lines, which can freely send and receive photos. The photos taken from this machine are almost as clear as negatives. Then we passed the entrance of the Editorial Department and visited in accordance with the newspaper production process. The work efficiency of each department is very high, the mechanical equipment is also very new, and the tidiness and cleanliness of the factory are particularly worthy of our admiration. In the vast printing room, twenty-one new printing machines are lined up one after another. At the front end, extremely long belts made of constantly rotating steel sheets receive the newspapers printed from each machine and transport them to the distribution department. Among the printing machines, there are four Asahi-style electro-optical rotary machines, which were custom-made based on the Asahi Shimbun's technical experience and have a particularly large printing capacity, capable of printing 160,000 large sheets of newspapers per hour. In addition, there are all American-style ultra-high-speed transfer machines.

After the normal tour, with the guidance of Mr. Hongo, we also visited the Editorial Bureau. Hundreds of people gathered in an extremely spacious hall, working separately. This is the busiest time for the Editorial Bureau, because the first edition of the next morning's newspaper must be printed by 8 PM, and sent by overnight train to distant places. After that, the edition must be changed at any time to insert newly arrived news. Most of it will not change (morning and evening editions are published many times every day, with the English letters on the newspaper corner indicating the edition). In our opinion, the vitality of their work function is simply comparable to the headquarters of a large army in modern warfare. They often send planes to distant places to investigate news, and use carrier pigeons to send letters to remote areas. They communicate with Tokyo and Fukuoka at any time through Asahi's dedicated long-distance telephone line. They are also in very close contact with other departments within the company. The Editorial Bureau is equipped with a vacuum transport machine that connects to many departments within the company. This machine is used to send manuscripts to the typesetting department. However, in a department like the Editorial Bureau, the spirit of work is ultimately more important than material equipment. Regarding this point, the impression we got was the orderliness of the organization and the strictness of the organization. In addition, we also saw four "Editorial Guidelines" posted in high glass frames on the wall for everyone to follow:

Asahi Editorial Guidelines (Translation)

First. With the aim of maintaining the eternal imperial foundation, we will strive for the peace of the country and the happiness of the people.

Second. We will guide the people's thoughts well, make the culture new every day, contribute to the prosperity of the national fortune, and accompany the progress of the world.

Third. Without bias or partisanship, we will not forget the concepts of fairness, impartiality, justice, and humanity. We will comment prudently and appropriately, and report accurately and quickly.

Fourth. The articles on the page should always be fresh, but we must also consider the impact on society. We will maintain a faithful and profound style, and never fall into frivolousness.

(Note) The organizational system of the Osaka Asahi Shimbun is listed as follows:

Sino-Japanese Economic Cooperation Underway, Japanese Troops Constantly Conducting Exercises in the Suburbs of Beiping, Preparations for the Construction of the Cangshi Railway, Japanese Military Attaché Discusses Economic Issues, Japanese Advisors Hired by the Hebei-Chahar Council

Beiping Correspondence: Since the stationing of Japanese troops in Beiping and Tianjin was completed, the Japanese soldiers stationed in Fengtai have been frequently dispatched in teams to conduct exercises in places such as Lugou Bridge, with a constant number of about one hundred people. On the 27th, several dozen Japanese soldiers stationed in Fengtai went to Beiyuan for exercises. At that time, a unit of the 29th Army was also conducting exercises in the same area. The two sides were very close, and conflicts almost occurred during their respective exercises. The Japanese side is expected to make some representations about this. The Foreign Affairs Committee also had a secret discussion on this matter during its regular meeting on the 28th. Subsequently, the person in charge of the committee explained everything to the Japanese side, and this matter is expected to be concluded. On the evening of the 28th, a Japanese elementary school student riding a bicycle on the Diplomatic Corps Street was beaten for not having lights and disobeying police orders. As a result, a small disturbance was caused, which has not yet been resolved, but it is not expected to cause a major problem.

Regarding the construction of the Cangshi Railway, the Hebei-Chahar Political Affairs Committee previously ordered Pan Yugui to be responsible for the preparations. The construction cost estimated by Pan is about 40 million yuan, while the railway authorities estimate it to be more than 30 million yuan. The Transportation Committee held its second regular meeting on the 28th and put forward this case for detailed discussion, but no concrete results have yet been obtained. The Economic and Transportation Committees are currently working together to devise a plan. However, this matter is also within the scope of Sino-Japanese economic cooperation in North China. Whether it will be handled independently by our side in the future, or whether it will have to wait for Wang Kemin to come north to negotiate joint operation with the Japanese side, is still uncertain. Mr. Wang was originally scheduled to return to Beiping in July, but due to environmental reasons, he failed to do so. It is difficult to predict when he will be able to come north in the future. However, it is heard that powerful figures here have made proposals for Mr. Wang to preside over the Economic Committee, and Mr. Wang is also concerned about the scope of the Economic Committee here, fearing that it will cause many inconveniences in future work. This is also one of the reasons for his delay in coming north.

At the reception with Chinese and foreign reporters on the 31st, Japanese Embassy Military Attaché Imai Takeo talked about economic issues. He said that the Japanese side hopes that China and Japan can promote economic cooperation and development. If this can be done, the Japanese side is willing to do its best to help. The Hebei-Chahar authorities are currently hoping to carry out work, and the Japanese side has expressed its goodwill towards them and is willing to help them achieve this goal. However, the economic development of North China is not possible with empty words. It must be promoted step by step. It is believed that our expectations can be achieved. It has not yet been heard where to start, but North China is the oldest land in China and has thousands of years of history. Therefore, if you want to do something, it must be in accordance with habits. If you do things in a special way, it may be difficult to achieve success. He also said that on the evening of the 29th, Chairman Song and Matsumuro Takayoshi invited Chinese and Japanese officers to a get-together, and on the evening of the 30th, there was a banquet for the Chinese and Japanese academic circles, which was of great benefit in spirit. My feelings about these two get-togethers can be summarized in two points: 1. Existing misunderstandings can be eliminated. 2. Psychology can be clarified and ideas can be connected. The Japanese garrison headquarters in Tianjin expanded its organization on the 1st. Kawabe and Matsumuro were both summoned by Japanese Army Commander Tashiro to Tianjin on the 1st for consultations.

The Japanese advisors hired by the Hebei-Chahar Political Affairs Committee are as follows: Nishida Koichi (former Consul-General in Jinan) as diplomatic advisor, Nakajima Daisaburo (Lieutenant Colonel) and Sakurai Tokutaro (Major) as military advisors, Saji Daiji (former Director of the Tokyo Telegraph and Telephone Bureau) as transportation advisor, ×× Takagi Daisan as advisor, and Yamazaki Ginji as Beining Railway Bureau advisor. It has been decided that Nishida and others will take office on the 1st.

Tianjin Customs Announces Trade Volume for the First Half of the Year: Imports Decrease, Exports Slightly Increase, Trade Deficit Exceeds 120 Million

Tianjin Communication: According to customs announcements, the trade volume in the first half of this year showed a sharp decrease in imports, which also led to a decrease in the trade deficit. In addition to affecting tax revenue, the foreign trade situation seems to be good. The import volume in the first half of this year was 45,900,000 yuan, the export volume was 33,271,100 yuan, the total import and export volume was 79,171,100 yuan, and the trade deficit was 12,621,800 yuan. Compared with the first half of last year, imports decreased by 15.9% (86,455,500 yuan), exports increased by 28.3% (73,342,000 yuan), and the trade deficit decreased by 55.8% (15,979,700 yuan). Compared with June last year, imports decreased by 8.5% in June this year (7,779,000 yuan), exports increased by 41.7% (17,777,000 yuan), and the trade deficit decreased by 49.6% (24,956,000 yuan). Compared with May this year, imports decreased by 1.5% in June this year (more than 1,340,000 yuan), exports increased by 4,265,000 yuan (equivalent to 7.6%), and the trade deficit decreased by 79% (more than 5,505,900 yuan). Kunshan Economic Construction Association Established

The branch of the National Economic Construction Movement Committee of this county has been officially established on the 1st after active preparations by the county government. Twenty-six heads of various agencies, groups, and schools have been hired as committee members, and twenty-four people including Wu Baofeng have been hired as commissioners. Chen Shouhe, Huang Zhenhuan, and Shen Guixiang have been appointed as secretaries, and Yang Chuanru has been appointed as director of the general affairs section. Chen Shouhe also serves as the director of the executive section. It has been determined that June 1st and December 1st of each year will be the dates for the general assembly.

Changshu Epidemic Still Prevailing

Although the weather here has recently turned cooler, epidemics are still being discovered, especially the Bie Luo Sha (sudden infant death) disease. Xia Zhixing, who lives in the Land Temple in the north gate, fell ill in the afternoon of the 1st. His whole body was ice-cold, and he died at about 4 o'clock, which was extremely rapid. Although the Public Security Bureau is planning to establish an epidemic prevention hospital, the budget expense of 650 yuan per month for the use of the reserve fund has not yet been approved by the Finance Department after being submitted, resulting in the delayed opening of the hospital. The public is eager for the hospital to be established as soon as possible to prevent the spread of the epidemic.

Car Station Chief Replaced

The Tanghu Automobile Company started operating on August 15th last year. Because the Changshu station controls the Shanghai, Wuxi, and Suzhou lines, the position of station chief was filled by Xie Xian, the younger brother of the Construction Department Chief Shen Baixian. It has been more than a year since then. Now, the company has transferred Shen to serve as the Shanghai station chief and dispatched Zhu Duanfu to Changshu to succeed him. The two sides are scheduled to take over the matter on the 5th.

Wuxi Three Fugitive Thieves Captured

The home of Chen Xiangchun, a resident of Chen Lane, Zhangjiaqiao West, outside the South Gate of the Second District, was robbed last year by more than a dozen thieves who took away a box gun, a pistol, and a rifle, as well as many bullets, 170 yuan in cash, and jewelry, resulting in huge losses. Subsequently, the Detective Team of the County Public Security Bureau cracked the case in Hushu Pass, Suzhou, and arrested four bandits, Tao Yalin, Chen Heshang, Yu Rengen, and Zhu Zengxiang. One box gun and one rifle were recovered and transferred to the court for interrogation and custody. Zhong Jihe, the captain of the Detective Team of the Public Security Bureau, continued to hunt down the fugitive thieves in this case. The day before yesterday, he led detectives Wang and Dai, as well as several detectives, to Youchepang, West Street, Hushu Pass, Suzhou. He remotely saw four small boats parked in a row, with bright candlelight in one of the boat cabins, offering sacrifices to the god horse, with three animals and fresh fruits. Captain Zhong and others rushed to ambush them. At that time, three male bandits, as well as women and children, were captured and bound. A Brownlin pistol was found in the cabin, which was the original stolen goods from Chen Xiangchun's home. They were all taken back to Wuxi, where the team interrogated them. The three thieves, Zhou Heshang, Chen Jinsheng, and Zhu Fusheng, confessed that they had robbed Chen's home. According to the confession, the County Public Security Bureau will transfer them to the court on the 3rd for interrogation and handling.

Guiding Autumn Silkworm Affairs

The autumn silkworm season is about to begin. The silkworm demonstration area in this county has prepared for autumn guidance. The locations and candidates for the guidance stations in each township have also been determined. A letter was sent to each guidance station the day before yesterday, scheduling them to report to the demonstration area on the 3rd. At 8:00 a.m. on the 4th, a departure guidance meeting will be held. On the 5th, they will all depart and go to each township to prepare for all autumn silkworm guidance matters. The date for the distribution of autumn seeds is approximately around the 20th.

Jiangyin Three Farmers Injured by Electric Shock

She Sanbao, She Fengbao, and Zhang Fubao, farmers in Dagojia Lane, Changshou Kunshan Township, Third District, were working on the mountain at about 4:00 p.m. on the 30th when a sudden thunderstorm struck. With a thunderclap, all three were electrocuted and fell to the ground. Sanbao's hair and pubic hair were burned off, and his chest was scorched. Fengbao's right eyeball was damaged and protruded. Fubao was less severely injured. All three were sent to the Dongwai Gospel Hospital for treatment. The lives of two of them are in critical condition.

Nantong Socialite Sentenced for Drug Trafficking

Fang Yu, a famous socialite in Tongcheng, was arrested by the Public Security Bureau for selling drug pills. The maid Chen Ma was also arrested. The two of them pushed the blame on each other, and the case was unresolved. The special commissioner's office is now clearing up the backlog of cases. The Provincial Government has dispatched Pan Bingying to Nantong to sort them out. Fang Yu and Chen Ma have each been sentenced to seven years in prison.

Court Promotion and Inspection Transfers

Hong Xiheng, a judge of the Nantong District Court, has been ordered to be transferred to the Shanghai District Court. Jiang Nongquan, a judge of the Qingjiangpu High Court, has been transferred to Nantong. Prosecutor Liu Shiqing has requested leave, and Lu Qi, a prosecutor of the Songjiang District Court, will temporarily replace him.

River Collapse and Embankment Breach Rescue

Tongyi has been experiencing violent storms and the river tides have risen sharply. The Yao Port river embankment has collapsed sharply. The residents of the polder are using sandbags to urgently block the breach and are working in shifts day and night to rescue it.

Zhenjiang New Grain Entering the Market Situation

The autumn rice harvest in the provinces of Upper Jiang is abundant, and rice boats are arriving in Zhenjiang one after another. The north of Jiangsu Province has also announced a good year. The new grain has already entered the market. Even the rice market in this city has seen a price drop, decreasing by about one yuan per stone compared to a few days ago. When the new rice floods in the future, the price will definitely drop sharply. As for the price of wheat, because of

the rain during harvest, the wheat was moldy, and the harvest was slightly inferior. Therefore, the drop is limited.

Yangzhou Court President Requests Resignation

Guo Wei, president of the Jiangdu District Court, requested his resignation from the High Court because he wanted to return to his native Changning, Hunan Province. Guo has now notified the accounting office to complete the handover procedures. However, it is not yet known whether the High Court will approve his resignation.

District and Town Conflict Case Transferred to the Province

Tang Zuomin and Wang Jiading, two assistants from the Fourth District Office of this county, brought along household registration police Hua Yizhi, Wu Xianjie, and Zhu Xiangzhong on the 18th of last month to collect the fourth installment of opium suppression licenses in Xiannv Town. When they checked the home of the opium addict Fan Jinhao, they saw Jiang Shoushan, an opium addict who had already quit. Tang and others believed that Jiang was suspected of relapse and that Fan was evidence of supplying people with opium. As a result, the two sides argued with each other. The town chief of the town, Wang Zhuyu, heard about it and brought along the town's militia to track them down and question Tang, asking why they brought so many people to the town day and night without notifying the town chief and entering people's homes to search. Therefore, Town Chief Wang believed that Tang and others were suspected of extortion and bribery, while Tang and others believed that Wang was guilty of obstructing official duties. As a result, the two sides clashed with each other, almost resorting to violence, and the situation was extremely serious. The county government heard the news and summoned both parties to the government for investigation for more than a month. Because the case was complicated, all the witnesses, including Tang Zuomin and Wang Zhuyu, were sent to the province the day before yesterday with a written statement. After careful investigation by the Zhenjiang Garrison Command, Wang Zhuyu was released on bail, while the rest were detained pending investigation.

Luhe Expedite Citizen Registration

The matter of citizen oath registration in this county was previously ordered by the Provincial Department to be completed by August 15th. Now, because the time is pressing, County Chief Qi convened a temporary meeting of district chiefs for discussion in order to actively carry it out. After the meeting, it was resolved that the deadline for investigating citizens would be August 4th, the deadline for citizen registration would be August 8th, the citizen oath date for each township would be August 12th to 14th, and the date for each district to report the number of citizens who have taken the oath and to send the citizen roster would be August 15th. After the resolution, the county government issued a notice to the district chiefs to comply with it.

Strictly Prohibit Performing Obscene Plays

In Houzi Township, Third District of this county, some people recently collected money to perform obscene plays. The county government has sent police to investigate and prohibit it. Unexpectedly, the villagers, without fear of the law, actually led a group of actors to hide in Donghe Township in this district during this investigation. Zheng Birong in the township took the opportunity to advocate collecting money from door to door and performing on a large scale. The local Bao chief not only did not stop it but dared to protect it. County Chief Qi learned that this was true through investigation and secretly dispatched the judicial police to rush to investigate and arrest them overnight. Zheng Birong, who took the lead, and the Bao chief who shielded the performance were arrested and sent to the case to be punished according to the law.

Hangzhou Reclaiming Sanmen Bay Project

To develop Sanmen Bay, the construction authorities have decided to first select those projects that are simple to construct and effective to implement. The plan to build a sluice gate and road in Che'ao Port requires 160,000 yuan, which can reclaim more than 5,000 acres of arable land, save about 60,000 acres of farmland water conservancy on both sides, and save about 15 kilometers of pond bank repair. The project is funded and constructed by the farmers themselves. It requires 28,000 yuan to build a dike, enclose the crossing, and set up sluice gates for cultivation. It can obtain 4,000 acres of mud land. Furthermore, the Jiangshan mud dike needs 11,000 yuan to build a dike and sluice gate, and reclaim more than 1,000 acres of mud land, which can be used as a small commercial port. The funding for other port water conservancy projects such as Yishi Jian Tiao Hu Zhu will be raised by the benefited farmland.

Fire Kills Four People

At 1:20 a.m. on the 2nd, the home of Zhang Guanzhao, a resident of No. 214 Xia Yangshi Street, Hangzhou, was destroyed by a fire caused by careless use of mosquito coils, which spread to the houses. Zhang, his wife, and son were all awakened in their sleep but could not escape in time and were burned to death. A 12-year-old girl from the opposite surname also died tragically in the fire. More than a dozen houses were burned down, with losses exceeding 30,000 yuan.

Ningbo: The Number of Smokers in the Anti-Smoking Center Increases Sharply

Since Yin County launched a general investigation into opium addiction on July 26th, all smokers found have been sent to the district anti-smoking center for verification. Moreover, the number of opium offenders sent from various counties has surged. The district anti-smoking center is already unable to accommodate them. Forty opium offenders were transferred to the detention center of the local court for custody. However, the number of arrivals far exceeds the number of departures, and there is still a feeling of not being able to accommodate them. Therefore, yesterday, eleven opium offenders, including Zhang Deren, who had already been sentenced, were temporarily released on bail.

A Woman in the Countryside Gives Birth to Quadruplets

In Zhongshan'ao, Lianshan Township, Fenghua, there is a farmer named Bao Lichen who married Chen from the same township. She is over twenty and has already given birth to a son, who is now eight years old. Last year, she became pregnant again and carried the pregnancy to full term. The day before yesterday, she experienced severe abdominal pain, and a midwife was called to assist with the delivery. After a short while, she gave birth to a daughter. However, the abdominal pain did not subside. Soon after, she successively delivered two more daughters and a son. The three daughters all died shortly after birth, while the boy's cry was very loud. Because the incident was unprecedented, it caused a sensation far and wide.

At 2:30 PM, detectives were dispatched, along with the Fourth Branch Bureau Chief and police, to investigate the address. Huzhou: Iron Ore Discovered in Changxing

Changxing is surrounded by high mountains and ridges, and its resources are very rich. The Changxing coal mine has long been mined, yielding considerable profits. Recently, another iron ore deposit has been discovered near the Lijiaxiang Shishan. After expert analysis, it is considered to have abundant components and excellent quality, and it is predicted that it can be mined for more than a hundred years. Bank of Korea: Expanding Operations in North China, Assisting Economic Development by Directly Circulating Japanese Currency; Japanese Military in North China to Make Water Conservancy a Prerequisite for Economy

Tianjin Dispatch: The Japanese Bank of Korea is expanding its operations in North China to complete its central economic development agency. The plan has been roughly finalized. However, in order to suit the deployment plan, Director Matsuyama has been specially sent to North China for inspection. Matsuyama came to Tianjin in the middle of last month and investigated in Tianjin for about a week. He has now transferred to Qingji and is scheduled to return to his country in the middle of this month to report to the head office. According to sources here, the Japanese side is quite concerned about the risks of investing in North China and is worried about any instability in the currency, which could affect the entire plan. Therefore, it intends to use the strength of the Bank of Korea to help make Japanese currency directly circulate within Hebei and Chahar, so that economic development can be guaranteed and the promotion of all enterprises can also achieve complementary effects. If this kind of conspiracy is realized, the so-called economic development of North China can achieve twice the result with half the effort. The Bank of Korea itself does not have this motive. It is entirely encouraged by the Japanese military. In the future, it plans to expand the original two branches in Tianjin and Qingdao into branches, set up branches in Pingji, and set up sub-branches in Tongzhou, Tanggu, and Tangshan. In addition to the purpose of promoting the direct circulation of Japanese currency in the market, it also operates savings, mortgages, and loans. Regarding this matter, according to observations in the Tianjin financial community, North China is a silver-using area, and its currency system has not deviated from the central government. Although there are now more types of paper money in circulation, they are all guaranteed by the legal currencies of the Central Bank, Bank of China, and Bank of Communications, and the people do not feel any inconvenience. If the Bank of Korea is allowed to circulate Japanese gold-based currency on the market, the result will be that the price of legal currency will be subject to fluctuating effects, and eventually it will become a case of the tail wagging the dog and being manipulated by others. Therefore, the authorities should pay serious attention to this matter and should not allow it to circulate vaguely.

The Japanese Garrison Headquarters in North China hired Dr. Sakamoto, a famous water conservancy engineering expert from Japan, several months ago, along with three of his assistants. After three months, they traveled to Baotou, northern Shanxi, Hebei, and Chahar, and inspected the upper reaches of the Yongding River, as well as the upper and lower reaches of the Hai River in great detail. Last week, they completed a dredging plan for the two rivers. After going to Jinan to meet with the Japanese Ambassador Kawagoe in Shanghai, he returned to his country. The Japanese Garrison Headquarters relies heavily on him and wants to use the plan he developed to first dredge the two rivers as a forerunner for developing the economy of North China, so that there will be no water disasters along the two rivers, and the effect of irrigation can be achieved through water conservancy. The fertile fields along the river can all grow cotton, and the Japanese textile industry can then obtain raw materials, which can be used inexhaustibly. The benefits of economic development can be enjoyed once and for all. Ishii, a senior staff officer of the Japanese Garrison Headquarters, once told Chinese reporters about this matter, saying, "Although there is talk about Sino-Japanese economic cooperation, no concrete plan has ever been drawn up. The Japanese Embassy and the North China Garrison Headquarters have not convened any meetings to prepare. Although the Japanese side plans to invest tens of millions of yuan in North China to develop mineral resources and water conservancy, if China, as the owner, is not willing to accept it, the Japanese side will not force it. Japan's real purpose is to restore North China to its prosperity ten years ago, and to restore the people's purchasing power to the past. At least they must have the same ability as the people of Manchuria, so that the Japanese economy can be developed and national defense can be indirectly consolidated. Dr. Sakamoto, the water conservancy expert currently hired by the military, has decades of water management experience. The Osaka water conservancy was built by him. After investigating the Yongding River and the Hai River, he said that he is very confident that he can manage them well. The military will definitely support his plan and take the lead." From this, we can see the direction of the Japanese side's emphasis on economic development. (August 1st)

Local News

The First Class of Trained Citizens in This City Held a Graduation Ceremony Yesterday Morning; Mayor Wu Gave Instructions Saying That There Are Two Purposes of Training: To Strengthen the Body and Develop the Habit of Discipline; A Total of More Than 4,500 Graduating Citizens

Central News Agency: The first class of trained citizens in this city held a graduation ceremony at Longhua Airport at 8:00 AM yesterday. It was not until after 10:00 AM that the ceremony was completed and dismissed. The details are recorded as follows:

Venue Arrangement

The ceremony was held at Longhua Airport. At the west end of the venue, three wooden platforms were set up, the middle one being the reviewing stand and the two sides being the guest seats. In front of the reviewing stand, a pair of couplets was hung, with the words: "Embodying the military in agriculture, industry, and commerce, the spirit of the Three Dynasties enhances our martial power," "The people are wise, benevolent, and brave; ten years of teachings have predecessors." On the guest stand, there was a horizontal banner each, one saying "Good citizens are the foundation of good soldiers," and the other saying "Good soldiers are the model of good citizens." The reviewed troops were all lined up in the center of the venue, extremely solemn.

Ceremony Ritual

Raising the flag, parade, march-past, commencement of the graduation ceremony, the chairman took his seat, the entire body stood in solemn respect, played music, sang the party song, bowed three times to the portrait of the Prime Minister and the portrait of Chairman Chiang, and the party and national flag, the chairman respectfully read the Prime Minister's will, issued certificates (played music), which were received by the captains of each battalion, awarded medals (played music), which were received by the captains of each battalion, the chairman delivered a speech, the officials delivered speeches, the guest representatives delivered speeches, the team members gave a reply, shouted slogans, took photos, ceremony completed.

Participating Officials

Those who participated in the ceremony included Inspector Mayor Wu, Accompanied Inspectors Wang Xiaolai, Cai Jingjun, Jiang Huaishu, Wang Shao, etc., Chief Judge Ji Jianzhang, Judges Zhang Tingrong, Wen Huazhou, etc., Commander-in-Chief Li Jiqi, Commander Tao Yi, and guests Chu Minyi, Yu Hongjun, Pan Gongzhan, Huang Boqiao, Xu Jinyuan, etc., more than 400 people.

Number of Graduates

The first class of trained and graduating citizens consisted of ten battalions, divided into thirty companies. In addition, there were many small teams of health, communication, locomotive, bicycle, and transportation vehicles. The total number of people was more than 4,500.

Assembly Slogan

The assembly slogans were: The military and civilians of Shanghai unite, support the revolutionary leader, implement the Three Principles of the People, revitalize the Chinese nation, Long live Chairman Chiang, Long live the National Government, Long live the Kuomintang, Long live the Republic of China.

Chairman's Speech

Chairman Mayor Wu said in his speech, "Distinguished guests, team members, today is the day of the graduation ceremony for the first class of trained citizens in Shanghai. This ceremony has given the 3.5 million citizens of Shanghai a profound impression and a new concept of the country. There are two purposes for the government to train citizens across the country. The first is to strengthen the physical fitness of citizens, and the second is to tell citizens across the country to develop good habits of observing discipline. These two purposes cannot be achieved without training. Everyone knows that to build a modern country is not something that can be done in a short period of time, nor can it be achieved by the efforts of a few people. To build a modern country and maintain national independence, it is necessary to have a strong physique and habits of discipline. Citizens are directly responsible for building the country. They have obligations to the country, and the country has rights to them. Citizens must first fulfill their obligations before the country has the right to give them. The greatest obligations of citizens to the country are military service, labor service, taxation, and education. If they can obtain the qualifications of citizens and fulfill these obligations, the country can be built and can survive independently. In order to strengthen the ability of the people to build the country and strengthen the ability to maintain national independence, the government has selected people with citizenship qualifications for training to strengthen their physique and develop habits of discipline. We know that to build a modern, independent country, individuals can enjoy a peaceful life and make the nation prosperous, and that it is impossible without every citizen fulfilling their due obligations. You are citizens, and the government wants you to participate in building a new country, so you are required to receive training. Training can not only increase the ability to build the country, but also increase the ability of the essence. You are engaged in agriculture, industry, and commerce in Shanghai. We must make efforts in our respective positions. In the future, the results will not only make our careers successful, but also have a great impact on society and the country. We must have a sound physique and a spirit of discipline in order to undertake major events and not be afraid of difficulties. Therefore, these two conditions cannot be lacking for your own careers. The customs and habits of the city are different from those of the countryside, so the physique and morality of urban citizens must be trained even more. After graduation, do not forget the lessons learned during the training period, and always maintain the spirit of training, so as to build the country, save the country from disasters, and make your own careers successful."

Guest Speech

Wang Xiaolai said in his speech, "I am very happy to participate in the graduation ceremony of the first class of trained citizens in this city today. I deeply hope that citizens with training qualifications will actively participate in the training, and I hope that all graduates will always maintain the spirit of 'straw sandals to save the country' today, and move forward in the mud to defend our country and be a model citizen." Chu Minyi then gave a speech, hoping for a consistent will and action, working hard to be self-reliant. Finally, the team member representative Tao Gongxuan gave a reply and dispersed.

Talk About the Grand Seventh Annual Meeting of the China Society for Arts and Sciences

Central News Agency: The seventh annual meeting of the China Society for Arts and Sciences has ended, and Chairman He Bingsong and Secretary-General Zhou Xianwen have returned to Shanghai. Silk Exports Expected to Increase Sharply

Commercial Inspection Bureau Inspects Grades; Can Compete with Japanese Silk

Raw silk was originally a major product of our country. However, due to backward production technology, Chinese silk has plummeted in the world market. Since the authorities have actively promoted reform, progress has been made and production has increased. Moreover, the consumption power of raw silk in various countries around the world has gradually increased again. Therefore, last year's silk prices rose, reaching a maximum of more than 1,000 yuan, which was rare in recent years. Therefore, the export of Chinese silk has also gradually turned for the better. According to the International Trade Bureau of the Ministry of Industry, observing the situation of the only raw silk consumer country in the world, the United States, last year Japanese silk imported into the United States was 46,124,600 pounds, an increase of about 5% compared to 42,238,000 pounds in 1934. The amount of consumption was 47,117,100 pounds, which was also an increase of 480,600 pounds compared to the previous year. Therefore, silk prices rose accordingly. As for the export of raw silk from our country, it has improved from extreme decline since the second half of last year, and exports have increased sharply. This year, farmers in Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces have increased silkworm farming and have a bumper cocoon harvest. The export of Chinese silk is also showing a booming trend. From June 1st last year to the end of May this year, 25,265 bales have been shipped to the United States, and the total silk export is 56,025 bales, an increase of more than 30% compared to the same period last year. In early July, foreign silk prices were affected by the good situation in the New York Stock Exchange, and silk prices rose day by day. This spring, rural areas in Jiangsu and Zhejiang were helped by loans from the Farmers Bank, and the road ahead was very strong. Silk prices are firm. If it is not affected by other factors, the future of the silk market this year is expected to not fail. However, attention should be paid to the inspection of raw silk grades. If the goods are uniform, they should not be affected by the exclusion of Japanese silk.

National Sugar Production and Sales Association Held Inaugural Meeting Yesterday; Retroactively Approved and Amended Article 21 of the Articles of Association; Three Internal Groups Started Working Immediately

After the election of directors of the China National Sugar Production and Sales Association, the association was originally scheduled to be established on August 1. However, due to the fact that Chairman Feng Rui was in Guangdong and could not come to Shanghai, the establishment was delayed. Now, because all parties are expecting the association to be established quickly, the board of directors decided to hold an inaugural meeting at the Dianchuntang Sugar Shop on Fuyou Road at 3:00 PM yesterday, chaired by Yuan Liang, retroactively approve the amended articles of association, and officially start working on the same day. The details are recorded as follows:

Attending Representatives

Yesterday, representatives from sugar factories in Guangdong, Guangxi, Sichuan, and Shandong provinces, the Shanghai Sugar Industry Association, the Sugar Industry All-Group Company, Xiehe, Heyuan, Yuansheng, Daxing, Yuda, Henghexing, Shenghe, Dachang, Yuantaiheng, Taiji, Shihe, Zhonghe, Yukang, Xiesheng, Yufengheng, Fangcuihe, Baohe, and Tongfengxiang and other sugar dealers, as well as the directors of the association, Yuan Liang, Lu Zuofu (represented by Zhang Shulin), Feng Rui (represented by Lin Qunyi), Zheng Zenan, Chen Yuren, Yang Wenshao, Lang Guangrui, Shi Yucun, Huang Jiangquan, Jiang Yachen, Chen Xinfu, etc., and Zheng Lai (represented by Huang Guoen), Director of the Customs Administration of the Ministry of Finance, Liang Hejun, Chairman of the Food Sugar Management Committee, Zhu Changnian, Supervisor of the Jianghai Customs, Wang Xiaolai, Chairman of the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, Yu Qiaqing, General Manager of the Sanbei Company, Chen Yiting, Member of the Municipal National Goods Promotion Association, and more than 100 people, and Yu Pu, Chief of the Yemiao Police Station of the Public Security Bureau, led police officers to protect the meeting.

Chairman's Speech

Yuan Liang was publicly elected as chairman and Xue Meiting was the master of ceremonies. After performing the ceremony, the chairman first gave an opening speech, saying that he was very honored that the association was established today and that the competent authorities and various groups had sent personnel to participate. Sugar is the second largest import of our country and is one of the necessities of life. The annual sales volume is about 20 million dan. In the past, most of it was supplied by foreign sugar. Now, our country, seeing the huge leakage every year, Guangdong, Guangxi, Shandong, Sichuan and other provinces have successively planned to set up mechanized sugar factories to recover interests. According to what I know, ten years ago, the statistics of sugar consumption in various countries, every year per person, the United Kingdom was 90 pounds, the United States was 70 pounds, Japan was 40 pounds, and China was 2 pounds. Recently, China has increased several times, so we must work hard to revitalize domestic sugar. The first is "production", and factories should be set up to improve manufacturing. The second is "sales", and we should find ways to promote sales. The purpose of this association is to seek the production of domestic sugar and develop sales power. I hope we will sincerely unite and jointly shoulder the responsibility of production and sales.

Preparatory Process

Then Zheng Zenan reported on the preparatory process, saying that in November last year, Feng Rui, Director of the Guangdong Forestry Bureau and General Manager of Guangdong Sugar, passed through Shanghai and talked with Shanghai sugar merchants about the proliferation of domestic private sugar and the increasingly dumping of foreign sugar, and that the sugar factories in Guangdong had gradually increased their sugar output, which had met the needs of the Chinese people. In order to prevent smuggling and dumping of foreign sugar, he proposed to form a production and sales group organization, which was supported by the government and prepared to organize the "China National Sugar Production and Sales Association." After active preparation, 14 people including Huang Jiangquan had been elected as directors of the association, and Feng Rui had been appointed as chairman. The articles of association consisted of ten chapters and twenty-five articles, which were passed by the general meeting of members on the 29th of last month and submitted to the Food Sugar Transportation and Sales Management Committee for registration and approval by the Ministry of Finance. The inaugural meeting was originally scheduled to be held on August 1, and Chairman Feng Rui was telegraphed to fly to Shanghai to preside over it. However, Chairman Feng Rui was busy with trading and could not fly to Shanghai, and various matters of the association needed to be handled quickly after the establishment, so the inaugural meeting was specially held today.

Retroactive Approval of the Articles of Association

Except for Article 21, all the articles of association of the association were passed by the general meeting of members on the 29th of last month. Now, Article 21 is specifically revised to "The resolutions of the general meeting of members of this association must be carried out with the attendance of more than half of the member representatives and the consent of more than half of the representatives. If the number of attending representatives is less than half, a provisional resolution may be carried out, and the results will be notified to all representatives. The general meeting of members will be reconvened one week later, within two weeks, and a resolution will be carried out on the provisional resolution with the consent of more than half of the attending representatives." The motion for retroactive approval was resolved to pass the original text. However, in order to avoid disputes between production and sales in the future, it will be submitted to the board of directors for research and remedy.

Speech and Notes

After passing the motion for retroactive approval of the amended articles of association, Liang Hejun, Chairman of the Food Sugar Transportation and Sales Management Committee of the Ministry of Finance, gave a training speech, saying, "I am ordered by the government to manage the transportation and sales of food, and I have unlimited feelings about the establishment of the National Sugar Production and Sales Association. I am impressed that sugar factories and sugar dealers across the country can unite and assist the government to prevent smuggling. After smuggling is eliminated, domestic sugar can be revived. Therefore, the government expects your association to succeed very much, and at the same time hopes to improve sugar making and sales, so that foreign sugar will not be dumped into our country's market again, which is fortunate for the country and fortunate for the people." Then Zheng Lai, Director of the Customs Administration, represented Huang Guoen and Yu Qiaqing Chen Yiting and others gave speeches, and the speeches were omitted for length. Finally, Yuan Liang gave a thank-you speech, photographed and had tea, and the meeting dispersed at 6 o'clock.

Official Office

The association is divided into three groups: general affairs, administrative affairs, and financial affairs. Lin Qunyi is the director of general affairs, Zheng Zenan is the director of administrative affairs, and Shi Yucun is the director of financial affairs. The association will officially start working today. The address of the association is in the Shanghai Sugar Industry Joint Company on Minguo Road. The association will issue a certificate to prove the legitimate transportation of domestic sugar after verification.

Three Tung Oil Experts Return to Shanghai After Inspection, Share Impressions of Tung Oil in Hunan and Hubei; Mr. Zhang Jiazhu Consults in Hangzhou

The Preparatory Office of the China Vegetable Oil Factory previously sent tung oil technical experts Lin Tianji, Wu Jinquan, and Liu Hu to Hunan and Hubei to investigate the general situation of the tung oil industry. They also visited Hankou, Changsha, and Changde. They returned to Shanghai on the 20th of last month. According to their written report, the following is an excerpt of their impressions:

Attitudes of Various Parties

(1) The governors of Hunan and Hubei provinces expressed great enthusiasm for the establishment of oil factories and provided detailed guidance and various conveniences. (2) Foreign oil refineries in Hankou were also willing to guide the tour and provide access for observation, which is greatly appreciated. (3) Foreign merchants suspect that the government will implement control over the establishment of tung oil refineries. (4) A small number of Chinese merchants, instigated by others, only care about immediate gains and do not understand the government's grand plan to improve tung oil, resulting in the same mentality as foreign merchants, and even instigating inland oil merchants, which is quite regrettable. (5) Inland oil merchants understand the overall situation, mostly support the factory's plan, and hope that the government will take effective measures against those who oppose it.

Trends in the Oil Industry

(1) In recent years, transportation has become more convenient, and the oil refining industry has gradually moved closer to the tung oil production areas, which can reduce transportation costs and taxes. Hankou is farther from the production areas, so many of the original oil refineries have been closed. (2) To improve oil quality and facilitate oil merchants, tung oil refining factories should be commonly established in tung producing areas, such as Chongqing, Changde, Yichang, Laohe, etc.

Improving Technology

(1) Hankou has always been a central market for tung oil. Currently, the oil refineries established by foreign merchants are limited to preliminary work, so the exported tung oil has not yet reached the level of refined and uniform quality, which needs to be improved urgently. (2) The traditional pressing method is inefficient and damages the oil quality, so it is necessary to switch to machine pressing. (3) The provinces of Hunan and Hubei have been promoting tung tree planting in recent years with great effort, but lack an overall plan and urgently need to adopt scientific methods to guide farmers to achieve practical results. The above points are just the main ones. It is said that the Preparatory Office has forwarded the details to the Ministry of Industry.

(Another Dispatch) Zhang Jiazhu, director of the Preparatory Office of the China Vegetable Oil Factory, and tung oil technical expert Liu Hu recently went to Hangzhou to meet with Wu Tingyang, director of the Construction Bureau of Zhejiang Province, to discuss a plan for cooperation between tung farmers and oil merchants in Zhejiang. Director Wu is very enthusiastic about helping tung farmers and has confirmed plans to establish oil refineries in Hangzhou and Wenzhou.

Japan Expands Banks in China: Taiwan and Korea Banks Seek to Control the Economy of Southern and Northern China

In order to control the economy of North and South China, Japan has decided to expand the Bank of Korea and the Bank of Taiwan. The Bank of Korea is designated to be responsible for North China, adding branches in important places in North China. The Bank of Taiwan is responsible for South China, adding branches in important places in South China. Therefore, our country's banks attach great importance to the expansion of the above two banks. A reporter from the Xinsheng News Agency has specially recorded the history of the two banks as follows: (1) The Bank of Korea was originally the Bank of Korea, established in 1909 with a special license from the Japanese government. In 1911, one year after Japan annexed Korea, the bank was reorganized and established as the Bank of Korea. The head office is located in Seoul, Korea. Branches in China include Shanghai, Qingdao, Tianjin, Andong, Dalian, Yingkou, Liaoyang, Shenyang, Xiaoxiguan, Tieling, Kaiyuan, Sipingjie, Changchun, Harbin, Lushun, Longjingcun, Fujia Dian, and Ge Yang, a total of 18 locations. The capital is 40 million Japanese yen, with 25 million Japanese yen already paid up. The public debt is more than 6 million Japanese yen. (2) The Bank of Taiwan was established in Taipei by Japan after the Sino-Japanese War and the Treaty of Shimonoseki, when Taiwan was ceded to Japan. It is a joint venture between the government and private merchants. It opened in 1899. The head office is located in Taipei. Branches in China include Guangzhou, Xiamen, Hankou, Shanghai, Shantou, Fuzhou, and Hong Kong, a total of seven locations. The capital is 15 million Japanese yen, and the public debt has reached more than 2.7 million Japanese yen.

The issue of levying income tax.

Shen Liren Expresses His Views

According to the Xinxin News Agency, the date for our country to levy income tax has been postponed again to September 1 due to the arduous preparation procedures. Shen Liren, an accountant in this city, expressed his views on the collection of income tax, which are recorded as follows:

Issues to Consider

The National Government included 5 million yuan for income tax in this year's budget. Although this number is not known on what basis it was obtained, given the large population and vast territory of our country, it is actually very small. However, this shows that our country is gradually moving towards the principle of equality in the taxation system, which is also gratifying. The date for the collection of income tax was originally set for July 1, but it has now been postponed again to the beginning of next month. The arduousness of the preparation work can be imagined. In the future, when collecting taxes, the procedures will be more troublesome than other taxes. Furthermore, the current collection of income tax is only for trial purposes. If the total revenue for this year is not enough to cover the expenses, will it be continued in the future? Considering the example of the United Kingdom, there have been cases where the cost of collecting taxes for the whole year exceeded the amount of income tax. This point should be considered by the preparatory authorities. It is said that there are 60 articles in the implementation rules for the new tax, but they have not been published. It is not known what their content is. As for the provisional regulations, the tax collection methods are divided into three categories: profit income, salary income, and interest income. The latter two are simpler in nature and easier to implement, so let's not discuss them for now. However, as far as profit-making businesses are concerned, there is much room for discussion. Gao Bingfang, Director of the Direct Tax Preparation Office, also expressed the same feeling. From the standpoint of a person engaged in accounting, I will present the issues that should be considered for the collection of income tax in our country at present.

Issue of Saving Expenses

(1) The issue of saving expenses. The opinion expressed by Finance Minister Kong in the newspapers the day before yesterday stated that the cost of collecting new taxes must be reduced as much as possible. However, according to Article 1 of the provisional regulations, the collection procedures for profit income must be divided into two steps. The first step is to calculate the percentage of income to the actual amount of capital. The second step is to multiply the prescribed tax rate by the amount of income to obtain the taxable amount. Therefore, the collection agency must also go through these two steps during the review. Taking Shanghai as an example, in the future, there will be hundreds of thousands of income tax report forms, so it will be necessary to hire many people to engage in this kind of review work, and expenses will not be saved. Moreover, from the surface, it seems quite fair to compare the actual amount of capital with the income to determine the amount of tax to be paid. In fact, those who run businesses should have a precise consideration of the amount of capital they need before they can determine it. The larger the capital, the more the income, and it is also very reasonable to levy taxes progressively. If the capital is large and the income is small, this is due to poor management, and the government does not need to specially reduce its tax rate. The payment of income tax requires filling out a report form. This kind of procedure is mostly done by the accountants of the taxpayer's business. The common format for the profit and loss statement in accounting is as follows: (A) Actual sales amount, (B) Subtract sales returns and discounts, cost of sales, (C) Gross profit, (D) Subtract various operating expenses, (E) Net profit. I believe that the classification of income tax report forms should be similar to the profit and loss statement, so that the accountants of each business can easily fill it out. The collection agency will save the labor of guidance and can easily review it, and expenses can be saved. The proposed format is as follows: (A) Total income, (B) Subtract tax-free portion, (C) Taxable income, (D) Subtract deductible expenses, (E) Taxable income. The classification of the above two tables is completely consistent. Taxable income is equivalent to gross profit, and taxable income is equivalent to net profit. Their meanings are very easy to understand and do not need to be explained.

Issue of Preventing Tax Evasion

(1) In addition to the issue of saving expenses mentioned above, how to prevent tax evasion is also very important. At this time when all industries are declining, with the implementation of the new tax, taxpayers are seeking ways to avoid or reduce taxes. If detailed regulations are not added, future tax revenue may be greatly impacted. Now, I will list the more important items in the following categories: (1) Actual capital amount. If the actual capital amount is to be used as a ratio with the income during collection, how the four words "actual capital amount" are to be explained is not specified in the provisional regulations. As far as we know, there are several types of actual capital amounts: original actual amount, net actual amount, and average amount. The calculation methods are different, and the ratio of income tax is also very different. Moreover, sole proprietorships and partnerships are more common than corporate organizations in our country, and their capital is not fixed and can be changed at any time, so that the ratio of income to capital is often less than 5%. In such a situation, what will the collection agency do? (2) Valuation of goods. Most countries adopt the principle of whichever is lower, cost or market price, for the valuation of goods. However, the market price of various goods is not uniform. Cunning people can reduce the valuation of their inventory, and the result will be less net profit, so they can avoid tax. Even if they have to pay, the amount will be small. Therefore, the implementation rules should stipulate that the valuation of inventory at the end of the period and the valuation of inventory at the beginning of the next period must adopt the same standard. Even if the taxpayer undervalues the inventory, resulting in less tax revenue, it can still be compensated for in the following year. (3) Tax-free portion. The interim regulations have stipulated some tax-free portions in Article 2, but attention should be paid to those who falsely set up various funds in order to evade taxes, such as labor compensation, old-age pensions, etc. The interest on these should also be added to the principal and managed by a committee organized by the workers themselves. (4) Deduction of operating expenses. According to Article 7, Paragraph 1, the income of the first category is taxed on the amount of net profit. Based on this, operating expenses must be deducted. However, how to deduct them is quite a problem. There are no provisions in the interim regulations for this point. Operating expenses can be divided into two categories according to their nature:

Types That Must Be Deducted

(A) Those that must be deducted: (1) Operating expenses whose amount can be determined: salaries, rent, advertising, water and electricity, and other fixed operating expenses. This type is easy to calculate and there are not many problems. (2) Operating expenses whose amount can be estimated: such as depreciation and bad debts. The level of their fixed rates is inversely proportional to the amount of net profit, so their impact is quite large. If the taxpayer arbitrarily sets the depreciation rate and bad debt rate high, the income from income tax will have to be reduced. The advanced countries in Europe and the United States that collect income tax have two methods to prevent this kind of tax evasion. One is to classify the depreciation rates of various assets and add detailed regulations, print them into a booklet, and issue them to taxpayers to follow. The other is to stipulate that once the depreciation rate and bad debt rate are determined, if the rate is reduced in the following year, the amount saved will be regarded as income and must still be taxed. On the contrary, it is regarded as a loss. For example, if the bad debt reserve for this year is set at 10%, totaling 1,000 yuan, and 500 yuan is recovered in bad debts in the decision year, this amount will be regarded as part of the income. After such regulations are made, disputes will be reduced. (3) Those whose amount is difficult to determine. In accounting, it is sometimes difficult to judge the difference between capital expenditures and expense expenditures. This kind of difficulty is also easy to encounter when preparing income tax reports. For example, machine repairs and partial replacements, etc., should they be deducted or not? The only solution is to treat them as expense expenditures and deduct them together with other operating expenses. If it is a capital expenditure, then in the United States and Europe, there are even detailed classifications of the repair and renewal expenses of various fixed assets, compiled into a booklet, so that auditors can use this to determine.

Types That May Be Deducted

(B) Those that may be deducted. Different countries have different regulations on whether or not to deduct this type of reward. For our country, we must examine the public sentiment, weigh the habits, and then make a decision. (1) Other direct taxes. Taxes can be divided into direct and indirect. However, it is not accurate to distinguish between the two. Generally, such as land tax, housing tax, income tax, inheritance tax, etc., are all direct taxes. So-called heavy taxes should refer to the same direct tax. The tax authorities should investigate whether there are any heavy taxes in the existing direct taxes. If there is a conflict with income tax, try to deduct it. (2) Insurance premiums. Fire insurance for houses should be one of the expenses. Life insurance is similar to savings and should not be deducted. However, the life insurance business in our country is still very immature. For the sake of promotion, it may be listed as a special deduction item. (3) Employee meals and lodging. In foreign countries, employees of ordinary businesses are generally not provided with meals and lodging. The situation in our country is slightly different. In the case of sole proprietorships and smaller-scale shops, employee meals and lodging are provided by the owners. In theory, only the employee's portion should be deducted. However, in fact, it is often mixed with the owner's meals and lodging expenses, and it is difficult to distinguish. Whether meals and lodging should be provided must also be stipulated. (4) Donations. Foreign countries generally exempt donations from tax. Wealthy people with large incomes are happy to donate. The United States has recently added a charity tax to direct taxes, so it is to prevent this kind of tax evasion. According to the situation in our country, whether to deduct it and how to prevent fake donations to evade taxes must also be considered. (5) Children's education expenses. Although Article 2, Category 3 of the provisional regulations stipulates that the interest on educational savings that does not reach 100 yuan per year is tax-free, should the expenditure on children's education also be deducted? In theory, the tax rate should be inversely proportional to the parents' income. Furthermore, for parents who are old and rely on their children for a living, a portion of their children's income should also be exempt from taxation.

District Offices Should Correspond with Organizations Using Official Letters

The National Federation of Chambers of Commerce telegraphed the National Government, the Executive Yuan, the Ministry of Interior, and the Ministry of Industry yesterday, saying, "We have recently received letters and telegrams from the Hankou Municipal Chamber of Commerce, the Henan Sheqi Cymbal Chamber of Commerce, the Hubei Ouchikou Chamber of Commerce, the Anhui Huoshan County Chamber of Commerce, the Hubei Pengyi Market Chamber of Commerce, the Jiangxi Leping County Chamber of Commerce, the Fujian Shangyang Town Chamber of Commerce in Yugan County, the Fuqing County Chamber of Commerce, and the Jiangxi Provincial Federation of Chambers of Commerce, etc., requesting to forward the request to withdraw the order of the district office to use orders for documents to agricultural, industrial, and commercial organizations. The district office and local industrial and commercial organizations are both people's autonomous organs. In the past, the use of official letters did not hinder the promotion of autonomy. If the district office must use orders, the good district head may not have any abuses, but the unscrupulous ones will inevitably abuse their authority over the local people, which may adversely affect the future of autonomous work. We hereby send this letter to your association, asking you to investigate and argue according to reason, and to withdraw the order of the district office to use orders for documents to industrial and commercial organizations, so as to value legal entities and prevent abuses, etc. Therefore, we hereby telegraph to your government and ministries for review and verification, and sincerely request that the order of the district office to use orders for documents to agricultural, industrial, and commercial organizations be withdrawn. In the future, official letters will be used for correspondence to prevent abuses. The National Federation of Chambers of Commerce of the Republic of China, Chairman Lin Kanghou.

Regulations on the Uniforms of Civil Servants, etc., Adopt Domestic Materials, Divided into Four Grades

Regarding the issue of unified uniforms for civil servants and military and political personnel, all using domestic materials, the Ministry of Industry has dispatched personnel to convene various manufacturers in conjunction with the Shanghai Municipal Social Affairs Bureau. The proposed domestic materials are divided into four grades: (1) Cloth: Cotton cloth woven from domestic cotton or yarn and domestic hemp textiles; (2) Woolen Fabric: Woolen cloth and serge woven from domestic wool yarn; (3) Silk Fabric: Silk cloth and serge and cocoon satin woven from domestic pure silk; (4) Dyes: Military training personnel use navy blue and light yellow uniforms, and civil servants (including judicial personnel) use black uniforms, and light yellow in summer, all using purely domestic colors. Samples have been made to Shen Xin, Wing On, and the Native Cloth Association and submitted to the Social Affairs Bureau for submission to the Ministry of Industry for approval, to be distributed to various agencies for adoption.

Narcotics Seized in Brothel; Proprietor Sentenced to Two Years

At No. 44 Xiaohuayuan Road, Zhejiang Road, someone secretly organized a human meat market (commonly known as a "salted meat shop") and provided opium smoking equipment. Customers with smoking habits could also buy and smoke opium at a considerable price. This was discovered by Western Detective Fang Te of the Flower Tax Squad of the Old Gate Police Station, who led Chinese Detective Zhang Jizhi of No. 1013 Hua Sandao to search the premises a few days ago. At that time, there were no prostitutes or customers, but two opium pipes, two containers of opium paste, one opium lamp, six ounces of red pills, thirty-one packages of raw opium, three containers of opium ash, and other smoking paraphernalia were seized. The proprietor, Shen Shousheng from Suzhou, was arrested and sent to the First Special Court. Wang Yaotang, a clerk from the police station, prosecuted him in accordance with Article 6 of the Opium Suppression Regulations. Shen also confessed that the opium was exclusively for customers to smoke when they came to the shop. After questioning by Judge Feng, the sentence was announced: Shen was sentenced to two years of imprisonment, and the seized smoking paraphernalia were confiscated.

Four More People Sue the Mei Hua Bank, Suing Gu Yubo and Others for Not Honoring Checks; The Court Must Investigate Before Further Hearings

After the Mei Hua Bank at No. 230 Jiujiang Road closed, lawsuits have arisen one after another. Now, Xiao Yuliang, Shen Enzhen, Luo Xiangsheng, Sun Chaoyong, and others have hired Lawyer Lin Zaoqing to file a complaint in the Civil Division of the First Special District Court against Gu Yubo, shareholder and manager; Zhang Xusheng, shareholder and deputy manager; Chen Yizai, shareholder; Bao Ziwen and Li Yijin, shareholder and director of affairs; and Wu Qinglei, shareholder and business director, for not honoring checks, and request a declaration of provisional execution. Xiao holds a Mei Hua bank check dated May 7 of this year, amounting to 7,000 yuan in national currency, while Shen, Luo, Sun, and others also each hold the bank's checks, amounting to 5,200 yuan in national currency, totaling 12,200 yuan in national currency. When they went to collect the money when they became due, they were not cashed. Although they have repeatedly reported it, they were ignored. The bank is registered in Hong Kong and has not registered with the National Government in accordance with the Banking Law, so it cannot be regarded as a legal person. Therefore, the shareholders are actually partners and should be jointly responsible for repaying all debts. Therefore, it is requested that they be ordered to jointly and severally repay 12,200 yuan, plus interest at the rate of 6% per annum until the date of repayment, and a declaration of provisional execution. Yesterday, the First Special Court held a hearing. After the plaintiff's lawyer stated the complaint, Qian Zheng, the clerk representing Zhang Xusheng, immediately stated that Zhang was not a shareholder of Mei Hua and that the plaintiff should provide conclusive proof. According to banking practice, checks cannot exceed a ten-day time limit, but the checks presented by the plaintiffs have a term of up to nineteen days. Moreover, there are multiple checks, all of which were issued when the bank collapsed, and the checks were issued in the name of Deng Gu Yubo, which is suspicious. The reason why the plaintiffs obtained the checks has not been explained. Therefore, it is requested that the plaintiffs be summoned to court to explain. The court verified the report and ordered a postponement for further hearings after investigation.

Chen Huizhang Case Support Association; Invited People from All Walks of Life Yesterday; Chen's Father Wept and Knelt Down, Begging

The Chen Huizhang Case Support Association, for the brutal murder of Chen Huizhang by British sailors, invited people from all walks of life yesterday. The rickshaw pullers' mutual aid association and the rickshaw pullers' association also hosted a large petition at the same time. The details are recorded separately below.

Attending Representatives

Yesterday at 2:00 PM, the Support Association invited people from all walks of life at the Jianghuai Fellow Association. Yang Chungkui of the Songhu Garrison Headquarters, Xing Hua of the Fish Market, Sun Choucheng of the National New Pharmaceutical Industry Association, Sun Zhaokang of the Yancheng Fellow Association, Zhang Wencai of the Lianshui Fellow Association, and Gu Jun, and others, totaling more than 400 people, with Su Chunlian, Zhang Shiying, Xu Yong, Wei Weiqing, and Li Longtu as the presidium. Zhou Weigao and others were sent by the Rickshaw Pullers Association, and Cang Gongwen, Xu Zhulin, He Wushan, Zhu Fengxiang, and other directors of the Rickshaw Pullers Mutual Aid Association, and more than a hundred rickshaw pullers went to petition.

Chairman's Speech

After performing the rituals, Chairman Su Chunlian reported, "We are very honored to have you here today for the reception of our association to people from all walks of life. As for the cause of this matter, it was very small, but the result was very serious. When this happened, three sailors were detained by the police station, but they were released without following the procedures. This is one point of disagreement. Also, because of the release of the three perpetrators, the identification of witnesses was resumed, turning the active criminals into suspects. Because they could not be identified, criminal charges could not be established, and civil charges were even more difficult to establish. However, the warship was willing to pay for the consolation, which is obviously contradictory. There are two ways to deal with this matter: (1) Punish the murderers in accordance with the criminal law for the public good; (2) Request consolation for the private good. However, this matter is of great importance, and it relies on everyone's wisdom and efforts to make a fair and just protest in order to achieve results. Therefore, I hope that all sectors of society will jointly support us."

Report on the Process

It was decided that Zhang Shiying would report on the process, advocating one: punish the murderers; two: consolation; three: apology; four: guarantee that similar incidents will not happen again. This matter is not just a matter for one person or one village, but a shame to the Chinese nation. Just like the case of Nakayama Hideo Hyosho, the Japanese attached so much importance to it, but Chen Huizhang also belongs to mankind, but he is ignored. Also, when the traitors in Tianjin were killed, the Japanese government demanded 30,000 yuan from us for consolation and 1,000 yuan for funeral expenses, but the Chen Huizhang case only offered 500 yuan. Why is the former valuable and the latter cheap? The organization of the Support Association is to fight for the entire nation," and so on. It was decided that Xu Yong, Li Longtu, Wei Weiqing, and others would give speeches, the main points of which were: (1) To persevere to the end and expand the organization; (2) To ask the authorities to observe the trial; (3) To comfort the family members and not be lured by money; (4) To recover consular jurisdiction.

Successive Speeches

It was decided that Gu Jun would speak briefly, saying, "I hope that your association's four goals will be resolved as soon as possible. If we do not achieve our goals, we will protest against imperialism. Do not forget that this is a means of imperialist oppression. The death of Chen Huizhang is a little blood of the Chinese nation." Yang Chungkui said, "I hope that we will not show weakness and jointly devise practical countermeasures to serve as a warning." Sun Choucheng said in his speech, "The death of Chen Huizhang is as light as a feather, while the deaths of Nakayama Hideo Hyosho and the traitors in Tianjin are as heavy as Mount Tai. You should know that the Chen Huizhang case is not a matter for the Jianghuai Fellow Association, but a matter for the Republic of China. Human beings should be equal, and we cannot ignore him just because he is a rickshaw puller and not an official." Finally, Sun Bawu and others spoke, with long speeches.

Now he has been innocently brutally beaten to death by foreign sailors. Such an act of overwhelming the host is not only contemptuous of the lives of the people, but also insults our national sovereignty. All compatriots cannot remain silent. We representatives feel especially concerned, since we are all subject to the same fate. At 3:00 PM on July 27th, we held an emergency meeting of rickshaw pullers at the West District Branch of the Rickshaw Pullers Mutual Aid Association, and decided on (1) punishing the murderers; (2) apologizing; (3) consolation; (4) guaranteeing that similar incidents will not happen again, and other matters, and designated Cang Gongwen, He Wushan, Zhu Fengxiang, and Xu Zhulin as representatives to send letters of support. Recently, we have learned that August 2nd is the date for your association to host a meeting with people from all walks of life to report the truth. We representatives are filled with grief and emotion. In addition to sending representatives to attend the meeting, we have also gathered our colleagues to petition the meeting, begging your association to uphold justice, argue on the basis of reason, and not stop until the goals of punishing the murderers, apologizing, consolation, and guaranteeing that similar incidents will not happen again are achieved, in order to protect national sovereignty and respect the lives of the people. The compatriots are fortunate, and the country is fortunate."
