The Chinese Buddhist Association Will Revise Its Constitution Again; The Standing Committee Notified Yesterday; The Supervisors Express Their Opinions

The Standing Committee of the Chinese Buddhist Association in this city sent a letter to all directors and supervisors yesterday, saying, "Respectfully, since the establishment of the association in the Republic of China in 1929, it has been six sessions until the summer of 1935. Because of being busy protecting the Buddhist property, the association has not been able to promote other important matters. The Buddhist associations in various provinces often did not report to this association when handling association affairs, and even the organization of Buddhist associations in cities and counties did not report for record. The membership fees that should be paid are mostly recognized but not paid, or not paid in full, resulting in an abnormal gap between the three-level Buddhist associations. The Buddhist associations in various provinces have failed to support the National Assembly at the top and failed to lead the cities and counties at the bottom. The handling of association affairs has not followed the right track, which is undeniable. Therefore, at the Seventh National Congress, in accordance with the central guidance for improvement, all guest Buddhist associations were abolished, and the city and county associations were used as branch associations, directly guided by this association, and the constitution was revised and submitted to the central party and government agencies for approval and record. Since the revision of the constitution at last year's congress, this association has been organizing and registering branch associations in accordance with the law.

Murder of a Seven-Year-Old Boy: Confession of the Criminal Obtained; Corpse Sent to Zhenru for Forensic Examination

Wang Zhanian, a 28-year-old man from Taizhou residing in a thatched shed along the road, more than a hundred paces north of Zhongshan Road on Hutai Road, Zhabei, worked as a refueling assistant at the North Railway Station. His elder brother, Changnian, lived with him. On the morning of the 25th of last month, Zhanian's eldest son, Yu Hong, only seven years old, disappeared while playing outside the house. The family searched without success and learned that he had been lured away by a neighboring boy named Gui Changyu. They immediately reported Gui to the Tanziawan Police Station under whose jurisdiction they fell, who transferred him to the Xinzha Sub-bureau, and then forwarded him to the Public Security Bureau. He was then escorted to the Shanghai District Court. The investigating judge ordered the plaintiff, Wang Zhanian, to bring Gui Changyu out and instructed him to find the child. Unexpectedly, around 4 PM on the 29th, a child's corpse was suddenly discovered in the Bai Pi Qiao River within the jurisdiction of the Pengpu Town Police Station.

The body was promptly retrieved and placed on the bank. The police station reported this to the Xinzha Sub-bureau, which notified the deceased child's father, Wang Zhanian, to identify the body. He confirmed it was indeed his son, Wang Yuhong, based on two small braids, a pair of small cloth pants, and a trouser belt. In addition to reporting to the Shanghai District Court for an autopsy, the plaintiff reported the

circumstances of the crime

to the Xinzha Sub-bureau. The Sub-bureau Chief secretly dispatched a detective squad, who successively apprehended five suspects. The statements of the defendant(s) are recorded as follows: The plaintiff, Wang Zhanian, stated that he lived in a self-built thatched shed in Guanyintang, Hutai Road. The shed consisted of nine rooms, which he shared with his elder brother, Changnian, who worked at a gas company for a living. Wang Changnian testified that

after the incident occurred,

Lu A'gen and Zhou Bingrong, who ran a small shop in the area, invited him to an empty house to discuss the matter, saying that Yang Jinbao, who was on the run, could find the child, but demanded a reward of 200 yuan, which was not paid. He did not expect that his nephew had already been murdered. The rest of his statement was similar to the above. The defendant, Zhou Bingrong, testified that he was 28 years old, from Funing, and lived on Hutai Road, working as a cart pusher. He initially denied everything but later admitted that he and the fugitive "Oldest" Yang Jinbao had a grudge against Wang Zhanian, and they planned to

lure the child out

and extort 200 yuan from him. However, they couldn't get the money and were reported to the police, so they killed the child and threw the body in the river wrapped in a reed mat. He also stated that he killed the child himself and that Lu A'gen and others were only watching. Lu A'gen testified that he was 20 years old, from Yangzhou, and ran a small cigarette and paper shop,

selling newspapers for a living.

He said he had to go to the newspaper offices at 5 AM every morning to pick up and distribute newspapers. He denied luring the child or killing him, but stated that he knew "Oldest" Yang Jinbao, Zhou Bingle, also known as Fan Dapeng, and Tan A'gen, all neighbors in the area. Fan Dapeng testified that he was 37 years old, from Funing, lived in a thatched shed on Hutai Road, and made a small living, as well as

being arrested for opium use.

Tan A'gen testified that he was 37 years old, from Shanghai, lived at 36 Guanyintang, and denied killing the child. He only admitted to knowing Fan and the others and admitted to smoking opium. Another person, named Mao A'wu, 34 years old, a local, lived at No. 10 Hutai Road and made a living by farming. He was

arrested along with the others

because he was playing at Fan Dapeng's house. However, according to the plaintiff, the deceased child was wearing a silver necklace and a pair of small silver bracelets, which were missing. When questioned, all the suspects denied any knowledge of them. The child's remains were incomplete, consisting only of the head, the skull split into two pieces, two small braids, a pair of small pants, a trouser belt,

several ribs,

and limbs that were recently lost. These remains have been sent by the deceased child's family to the Zhenru forensic examination office, transferred by the Shanghai District Court, awaiting examination. The defendants and the victim's family have been escorted by the Xinzha Sub-bureau to the Public Security Bureau, awaiting transfer to the Shanghai District Court for trial.

Zhong Boliang Accused of Forging Promissory Notes

Zhong Boliang, a native of Pudong residing at No. 439 Zhaozhou Road, Tangjiawan, had previously used an 84-yuan promissory note from Chunyuanzhuang, dated June 30th, to Ningbo native Chen Mingyong. Falling from the Fifth-Floor Roof: Shop Assistant Dies Tragically; Right Hand and Right Foot Bones Broken; Internal Injuries Cause Instant Death

Chen Siliuzi, a young man from Yangzhou, 18 years old, worked as a junior shop assistant at the Chen Sentai foreign iron shop located at No. 35 Molin Street in the French Concession. He earned two yuan a month after completing his apprenticeship. Yesterday morning at 8 AM, he and his fellow apprentice, Dong Wenyuan (19 years old, also from the same hometown as Chen), were repairing a leaky lead roof on the fifth floor of the Changsha Merchants' Guildhall at No. 2 Diandang Street outside the Old North Gate. Unexpectedly, Chen accidentally slipped and fell from the roof to the ground, resulting in broken bones in his right hand and right foot, a cut on the left corner of his mouth causing bleeding, and internal injuries from the impact. He died instantly. The Changsha Merchants' Guildhall reported the incident to the Daxizi Clock Meilan Police Station, which sent detectives to investigate. The body was transported to the Tongren Fuyuan Branch Hall for autopsy, pending a court-appointed examiner today.

Refugees Passing Through Must Have Passports from Their Original Counties; Otherwise, Passage Will Not Be Allowed

In recent years, the provinces of Henan and Shaanxi have suffered from floods and droughts, and people in various regions have suffered from famine, with starving people everywhere lacking food and clothing. The strong form groups and go to neighboring provinces to beg for food. It is difficult to distinguish between good and bad among them. The Jiangsu Provincial Government, considering that these refugees are of mixed quality, in order to avoid affecting social order, took preventative measures. Yesterday, they specially issued an order to the Shanghai County Government that, in the future, if starving people or large numbers of refugees pass through seeking a living, they must have passports from their original counties before they will be allowed to pass. Otherwise, passage will not be allowed. If they linger within the borders, the police are authorized to escort them out of the borders to avoid causing disturbances.

Qingliang Temple Property Dispute: Partial Execution of Old Buildings Today; Valuation and Purchase of the Entire Property Underway

The property dispute involving Qingliang Temple and the mortgagee, Sheng Yulin's Tonghe Foreign Firm, has been in litigation for several years. The court ruled in favor of execution, but public opinion opposed the mortgaging and sale of religious relics in order to preserve the temple property. Therefore, local people organized a support association and initiated administrative remedies, leading to delays until now. Last week, the court reopened the debate and advised both parties to reconcile, but to no avail. Therefore, it was decided that at 9 AM today, the execution of several old buildings next to the temple, a dozen or so rooms, will be allowed first. As for the relocation of the rest, a grace period will be granted to find a way to negotiate. A reporter from the Huadong News Agency inquired with Qinghai, the abbot of the temple, who said that the temple is a local public property and a religious building. Because Tonghe has not been sincere in negotiations, it has been impossible to resolve the matter. As for the more than ten old houses that were executed today, the temple had already renovated them at a cost of millions. If Tonghe repays this cost, it will be difficult to dispose of this property. The Maintenance Committee's intention is to purchase the entire temple property from Tonghe at the price stipulated by the Public Works Department, which may be a solution. This is currently underway, but the outcome depends entirely on whether Tonghe is sincere in resolving the dispute. Therefore, although it is called execution now, it actually cannot resolve this dispute.

Robbers Identified by Accomplices

Pan Hongyu's cigarette and paper shop at No. 37 Kunming Road was closed and locked at 10:45 PM on October 19, 1933. Unexpectedly, five robbers armed with weapons broke in and tried to rob the shop. Unable to open the iron gate, the shop assistants sounded the alarm, and the robbers fled in different directions. Subsequently, the Hongkou Police apprehended four robbers involved in the case: Han Songlin, Tao Jingen, Tang Jiquan, and Liu Heshang, and sent them to the First Special Court. After interrogation, they were sentenced to prison and are currently serving their sentences. The accomplice who supplied the guns for the case, a Ningbo native named Lu Gencai, remained at large. Until last winter, he was arrested for another robbery and sentenced to eight years in prison. Recently, Cui Chengke, a Chinese detective from the Huishan Police Station, learned of this and went to the prison to have the four robbers, Han, etc., identify him as their accomplice. He was brought back to the police station the day before yesterday. Yesterday, he was escorted to the Third Criminal Court. Zhang Shizhu, a lawyer from the Public Works Department, described the incident and presented evidence from the convicted robbers Han, Tao, Tang, and Liu, proving that Lu initiated the plan, provided the money to buy the guns, and went to rob the shop. When questioned, Lu made evasive statements. Judge Xiao sentenced Lu Gencai to three years in prison as a warning.

Private Prosecution Cases Still Received Directly by the Court; However, the Reasons for New Cases Should Be Simultaneously Sent to the Prosecutor to Prevent Abuses Such as Filing Both a Private Prosecution and a Public Indictment

The President and Chief Prosecutor of the Shanghai District Court recently received instructions from the Jiangsu High Court, stating that: "The Department of Judicial Administration's Order No. 3360 was received. The Chief Prosecutor of the Hunan High Court reported, 'The private prosecution system was originally intended to reduce complexity and improve litigation. Since its implementation, private prosecution documents have been directly received by the court. There is no communication between the court and the prosecutor. Cases have occurred where private prosecutions are filed before the prosecutor concludes the investigation of a public indictment, or private prosecutions are filed after disposition, or public indictments are filed while private prosecutions are underway, or even the same case involves both private and public indictments. Because the court and the prosecutor have separate jurisdictions, and the facts often differ, they handle cases separately, leading to confusion. It is only after the fact that the issues are discovered and corrected, resulting in repeated delays and litigation burdens. This not only harms the people but also undermines the dignity of the law. I have repeatedly considered this and respectfully request that your department issue an order to all courts that, in the future, private prosecution cases be received and transferred by the prosecutor, so that the provisions of Articles 315 and 316 of the Criminal Procedure Law can be easily implemented, and the above-mentioned abuses will not arise. All information regarding the implementation of the private prosecution system and its remedial measures are hereby submitted for your review and implementation.' According to this, it is true that failing to communicate between the two parties in private prosecution cases makes it difficult to avoid the various abuses mentioned in the original report. However, if all private prosecution documents are received and transferred by the prosecutor, it would not only increase the burden, but also make it easier to confuse private and public indictments. The court should continue to receive them directly, but whenever there is a new case, the reasons for the case should be sent to the court's prosecutor for review to remedy situations where a private prosecution is filed before a public indictment is concluded, or a private prosecution is filed after a public indictment is disposed of, or both a private prosecution and a public indictment are filed simultaneously, or a case involves both private and public indictments. Please comply with this order and instruct your subordinates to do the same." Upon receiving this order, the President and Chief Prosecutor of the court are to be instructed to comply. This is the order.

Land Measurement Begins in Luhang and Gaohang

The Shanghai Municipal Land Bureau posted Public Notice No. 15 yesterday, stating that, in order to measure the land in Blocks 8, 17, and 18 of Section 22 of Luhang District, and Blocks 52 and 53 of Section 22 of Gaohang District, landowners should fill out and claim measurements. The Bureau is now beginning to measure the land in Blocks 8, 17, and 18 of Section 22 of Luhang District, and Blocks 52 and 53 of Section 22 of Gaohang District. Landowners should pay attention to the following items: (1) The land chief will distribute reporting forms to landowners. Landowners should fill them out truthfully within ten days of receiving the forms and have the land chief collect them and deliver them to Surveying Team No. 1 at No. 26 Zhangjiaqiao Town East Road, Luhang District, or landowners can deliver them to the surveying team themselves. (2) If landowners do not receive the reporting forms because their addresses are unknown, they can fill out the forms themselves at the Bureau or Surveying Team No. 1. (3) If landowners cannot fill out the field list name and acreage because the field lists are mortgaged, they should immediately copy them from the pawnbroker and not refuse. (4) When the land is measured, landowners must, together with the land chief, clearly point out the boundaries to the surveyors.

Or pre-authorize a representative to identify the boundaries. Otherwise, the Bureau will only rely on the land chief's instructions, and landowners will be responsible for any errors that occur in the future. The above four items are related to landowners' consolidation of property rights. In addition to instructing the land chiefs in each block to comply, it is necessary to issue a public notice so that landowners pay special attention. This notice, also serving as the director, Xu Fu.

Economic Supplement

The Recent Trend of Prices and Their Future

— Zixiao

Since 1931, China's prices have fallen rapidly; among the ups and downs of various prices, there is a regular development, that is, the decline in export prices is faster than wholesale prices, and the decline in wholesale prices is faster than import prices. Therefore, the difference between the three gradually increases, forming a regular sequence. If the indices of the three types of prices are plotted on a line graph, the sequence is clearly displayed on the graph. Although the trends of the three are similar, there is a great difference in degree. This difference shows the extremely unfortunate fate of the Chinese economy. Under the double pressure of overseas devaluation and rising silver prices, in order to maintain its only point of export in the international market, China had to try its best to suppress export prices so that the sales price of export commodities abroad could be in harmony with international prices. In this way, the export prices had to be suppressed lower and lower, and the terms of trade—the rate of barter—became more and more unfavorable. Farmers used to be able to exchange ten catties of fertilizer with one and a half days of labor, but in the summer of 1935, they had to spend two and a half days of labor to exchange the same amount of fertilizer. This is the so-called exploitative terms of trade. Since the currency reform in November of last year, the situation has been completely reversed. We abandoned the old silver standard, and the exchange rate suddenly dropped by more than 40% in the night of November 3rd to 4th and was stabilized. Prices were no longer dominated by the rising exchange rate but were turned to be affected by the sudden decline in the exchange rate. As a result, all kinds of prices tended to rise together. The depressed national economy, on the road of traveling in the underworld, received extraordinary stimulation, and there was a temporary appearance of excitement. The return of the national economy from adversity seemed foreseeable. However, the rise in prices and its trend since August have two facts that are generally noticed. First, the most severe rise in various prices was only in the one or two months after the currency reform, namely November and December of last year. In the following months, the rising trend was weakened, showing signs of stagnation. Second, the degree of rise in various prices was quite different from each other. At the beginning of the currency reform, the highest increase was in import prices, followed by export prices, and then wholesale prices and the cost of living index. The trend in the following months was quite different. Export prices continued to rise, while import prices, after a period of exuberance, felt hesitant and showed signs of retreating. If the three types of prices mentioned above are plotted on a graph, the trend is not as regular as before the currency reform. Wholesale prices and export prices rise together, while import prices show a slight decline, with no stable relationship. The following are the indices and situations of export, import, and wholesale prices:

Although the degree of increase in export prices and wholesale prices at the beginning of the currency reform was not as high as that of import prices, they later showed a trend of gradual increase. Although the rise in import prices was more rapid at the beginning of the currency reform, they later showed signs of stagnation. The explanation for this phenomenon is quite noteworthy. A group of blind scholars believe that although prices had a sudden rise during the currency reform last year, they later showed signs of stagnation and did not continue to soar. Therefore, they frequently issued pessimistic arguments. This is superficial talk and need not be discussed. They only know that China's exchange rate has been devalued, but they forget that China's exchange rate was immediately stabilized after being devalued by 40% in one day and night. They did not consider whether a sudden price surge is needed under a stable exchange rate. The views of another group of people are more progressive. They believe that after the currency reform, export prices rose the fastest and maintained a continuous upward trend, import prices were more stable than export prices, and wholesale prices and the cost of living index were more stable than import prices. Therefore, they put forward optimistic opinions, saying that China's terms of trade—the rate of price exchange—will become more and more favorable, and people can exchange the same amount of foreign goods with less labor. The exploitative exchange rate will no longer be a disaster for China's economy. Secondly, farmers, who are producers of raw materials, will see their economic situation gradually improve under the circumstances of rising export prices and favorable terms of trade, and their benefits will be greater than those of other classes. The income of the largest majority of people in the country will increase more than before, and the prosperity of the national economy is even more promising. Therefore, they seem to hope that export prices will continue to be in the leading position of rising, because this is the way to increase the income of raw material producers and make the terms of trade more favorable. Although this view is more insightful than the previous one, it is still open to discussion. Below, we will try to analyze our opinions on the current situation of price trends.

First, under a stable exchange rate, there is absolutely no need for a drastic change in prices. This reason is very simple, and everyone with common banking and monetary knowledge understands it. Since the exchange rate is stable, if prices rise too quickly, or even without a certain limit, it will be difficult to export goods, the balance of international payments will be affected, and the stable exchange rate will be subject to reverse adjustment, and even collapse because it cannot maintain its stability. The theory is like this, and recent international events can be cited as evidence. The most important point of the strength of the pound is that domestic prices can be maintained stable. We assume that if domestic prices in the United Kingdom suddenly rise by 10% or 20% in the short term, we dare to assert that the British government and the public will not be happy about it, but will suddenly feel the difficulty of maintaining the pound price. The most important point of the recent repeated crises of the franc is not the decline in prices, but that under the circumstances that the French government is trying to tighten up in order to make export prices in line with international prices, suddenly prices rise in the opposite direction, making France's international payments even more trapped in a desperate situation. We assume that if domestic prices in France rise by another 10% or 20% in the short term, the price of the franc will inevitably collapse, and the situation will be as clear as watching fire. The recent events in these two countries can be used as our reference. The stability of prices is a prerequisite for the stability of the exchange rate, and the situation in our country is the same. Although our country's exchange rate has been devalued by 40%, it is now kept fixed and not allowed to fluctuate slightly. If domestic prices suddenly rise by 50%, it will be more difficult to export goods than before the reform, and it will be easier to import foreign goods than before the reform. Its advantages and disadvantages to our country's economy are self-evident. Therefore, we are not worried about the fact that prices have not changed drastically in the past few months, and we secretly congratulate ourselves, thinking that this is the best phenomenon. I hope that the people of the country will not be deceived by fallacies, thinking that with a little effort, prices can rise to the sky. If prices rise too quickly, not only will the exchange rate be affected by reverse adjustment, but also domestic credit will expand, the distribution of benefits will be uneven, and a phenomenon of profit inflation (Loflation of profits) will be created, which will not only not help the national economy, but also sow the seeds of new panic. In the future, we only hope that prices can rise slowly in stability, which will be the most beneficial contribution to laying the foundation for national currency credit and adjusting the domestic economic structure. A galloping price change is not only not welcomed by us, but should also be avoided with all our efforts.

Second, there is also a certain limit to the degree to which export prices rise faster than import prices, which is beneficial to the national economy, and this situation cannot be allowed to develop indefinitely. Before the currency reform, export prices fell the fastest, making our terms of trade in international trade increasingly unfavorable, which was generally recognized as an exploitative mode of trade. Since the currency reform, although the changes in export prices in the first one or two months were not as fast as those of import prices, in the following months, import prices showed signs of stagnation, while export prices showed a trend of gradual rise. This development, as the optimistic interpretation suggests, our terms of trade are gradually turning to be favorable. The income of raw material producers has the possibility of increasing proportionally. However, we believe that this issue should be viewed from another aspect. If import prices remain relatively stable, and other domestic prices gradually rise, as shown by the domestic situation in the past few months, then there is a big question whether it is possible to increase imports. Assuming that there are no major changes in foreign prices and our exchange rate is fixed, then it can be asserted that there will be no major fluctuations in import prices. Import prices do not change due to the stability of the exchange rate, while the general price level in the country gradually rises. The meaning is that the sales of foreign goods are more convenient. If there is no other factor at work, it is inevitable that imports will increase and the balance of international payments will turn to be unfavorable. This is one. Secondly, export prices rise day by day, and the exchange rate has been fixed. The meaning is that the selling price of our country's goods abroad gradually rises, and the result will inevitably affect our country's export trade. This is also a question. Under the circumstances that the exchange rate is fixed and export prices rise, if there is no other special force at work, it is inevitable that the export capacity will be weakened as a result. We further compare with the specific situation in our country, which makes us have to have this suspicion. Let us now look at the extent of the rise and fall of prices in June of this year and the same period last year:

The export price in June of this year was 27.1 percent higher than in June of last year, while the import price only rose by 18.6 percent. Wholesale prices rose by 14 percent, and no other country in the world has risen as fast as ours. Export prices should theoretically be in line with international prices, and the result of rapid increases will inevitably lead to a loss of balance with international prices, making our country's international trade also tend to be unfavorable. This is a very possible trend. Looking at the recent international trade situation, we have to have this worry. For example, the export index of agricultural products once jumped to above 100 during the currency reform, but now it has fallen to between 60 and 70. Therefore, we believe that under the circumstances of a stable exchange rate, a continued rise in export prices is by no means beneficial without any drawbacks. If there is no stable solution, it is feared that it will be a hidden danger for the future.

In short, in our opinion, although prices rose once after the currency reform, they immediately maintained a considerable degree of stability. This is indeed a gratifying phenomenon. What we hope for in the future is still the steady stability of prices, and absolutely not galloping prices. As for export prices leaving import prices and continuing to rise on their own, we also recognize that it is beneficial within an appropriate limit, but if the trend remains unchanged for a long time, the result may inevitably affect our country's international balance of payments. It seems that we should not hope for high prices today, but should hope for the stability of export prices and the general price level. The government's policy should also be based on this point. Here, we want to add a warning that the stability of prices is a necessary condition for the stability of the exchange rate. In order to seek the stability of prices, the issuance of legal currency must be repeatedly cautious.

The Essence of China's Cooperative Movement

— Chen Zhongming

—And the Mission It Bears—

I.

The cooperative movement is a product of the ailments of capitalist society, which have already taken shape and are increasingly exposed. The maladies of capitalist society, in economic form, are exposed as the threefold contradictory phenomena of "inequality," "insufficiency," and "instability." Once this phenomenon envelops the entirety of capitalist society, the bright and brilliant golden world of capitalism immediately transforms into a dark hell of panic, war, carnage, unemployment, hunger, and death.

The cooperative movement is one of the various methods to save this tragic fate. Advanced cooperators, from the perspectives of ethics, sociology, and economics, recognize the cooperative movement as the only way out for human society. Only by managing society and the world with cooperative qualifications can humanity step into a peaceful and beautiful "world of great harmony."

This extremely grand ideal and goal are undoubtedly worthy of our admiration. However, no two countries in the world have completely identical historical backgrounds, nor do they have completely identical social systems. Social movements arising from different historical backgrounds and different social systems naturally cannot have completely identical standard models. Secondly, the establishment of a social movement theory is initially an attempt by some great seers or progressive scholars and theorists, inspired by objective facts and lofty ideas, to create a grand worldview. However, due to differences in the objective things that each person perceives and the research methods adopted, even though they start from the same starting point, the results are vastly different.

The paths taken by cooperative movements in various countries around the world, as mentioned above, have evolved into the current complex and uneven situation, either due to different national conditions or due to differences in the viewpoints of leaders.

The cooperative movement in capitalist countries is merely a tool to appease farmers and workers, avoid panic, and alleviate social revolution. The cooperative system it adopts is an appendage form based on capitalism. The cooperative movement in socialist countries takes socialist economic construction as a prerequisite, and in terms of development steps, it is a concession to the communization of backward rural areas. In addition, pure cooperativists, due to differences in viewpoints and theories held, have distinctly formed two camps: the consumer faction and the producer faction.

Since the cooperative movement in various countries around the world has such divergent and complex trends, it is essential to conduct a concise review of the theoretical basis of the various trends mentioned above before deciding which cooperative system China's cooperative movement should adopt.

II.

The field of economic research usually includes four sectors: production, exchange, distribution, and consumption. It was only recently that these four sectors were fully enriched in economics. Adam Smith only paid attention to production and exchange. Malthus and Ricardo began to pay attention to distribution. Marx negated the production of capitalism from the development of production, exchange, and distribution. Since the marginal utility school, the subject of consumption has been regarded by scholars as a proposition that should be strictly noted. This evolution in the history of doctrine is, in fact, the corresponding reflection of the evolution of economic history.

The highest goals of the consumer and producer factions of the cooperative movement are not necessarily different; the difference lies only in the starting point. The consumer faction recognizes consumption as the purpose of economic life, and production is merely a means to satisfy this purpose. Therefore, consumption behavior is a universal behavior that everyone must possess. As a result, the consumer camp has an absolute majority compared to the producer camp. Consumers in capitalist society are completely dominated by specific production relations, and the oppressed and the sacrificed are the large groups of consumers. Only when consumers organize themselves and manage production in a planned and methodical manner can the maladies of capitalist society be eradicated. Therefore, the cooperative system advocated by the consumer faction, under the four principles of making the best use of things, making the best use of talents, abolishing profits, and satisfying needs, develops consumer cooperatives, organizes wholesale cooperatives, and then directly establishes production enterprises to complete the ultimate goal of consumers managing production.

As for the theory of the producer faction, it retains many sentiments of French utopian socialism and British Christian socialism. Fourier wanted to create another "phalanstery" production organization to replace the contradictory society of oppression and resistance, thus pioneering French production cooperation. Christian socialists, from a doctrinal and ethical perspective, sympathized with the poverty and lowliness of the working class's life, believing that workers could only enjoy human happiness by organizing production cooperatives.

In addition, the cooperative systems adopted as policies by capitalist countries and socialist countries are either a temporary appendage under the inherent system or a temporary transitional bridge before the ideal system can be realized immediately. Socialist countries have their unique political institutions to manipulate freely. It goes without saying that the cooperative system of capitalist countries cannot develop into a general main and central social system.

III.

China's cooperative movement should be the cooperative movement of the Three Principles of the People. The Three Principles of the People is the only doctrine for solving all revolutionary problems in China. "The primary task of national construction lies in the people's livelihood." The philosophical foundation of the Principle of People's Livelihood lies in the historical view of the people's livelihood. Therefore, the foundation of China's cooperative movement should also be placed on the people's livelihood.

Accordingly, "life" is the ultimate purpose of humanity, and consumption and production are merely two processes of a means adopted to satisfy this purpose. Therefore, from the standpoint of the Three Principles of the People cooperative movement, consumption and production should be unified in the same entity of the Three Principles of the People cooperative movement, and should not be arbitrarily divided into two opposing camps of producers and consumers, which is to demand the coordination of consumption and production to complete the entire solution of the people's livelihood problem.

Secondly, China's cooperative movement is a movement for the economic autonomy of the nation. The oppression suffered by the nation is mainly the economic oppression of the imperialists. As a result of the economic aggression of the imperialists, China's society as a whole has fallen into a deep abyss of panic. The mission of China's cooperative movement is to bear the burden of establishing China's independent economic unit and strive for the economic autonomy of the nation from the international imperialist economic aggression. Furthermore, China's cooperative movement is the backbone of the national economic construction movement. China's production is backward and needs to engage in the national economic construction movement. This is essentially different from the social reform movement of capitalist society, which has reached the extreme of production and only requires solving the problem of distribution and consumption. Therefore, the mission of China's cooperative movement is to build economic national defense and defend against aggression on the one hand, and to develop production enterprises and strive for self-sufficiency on the other hand. Under this goal of economic construction, increasing agricultural and industrial production has become a decisive prerequisite. To break the gap between urban and rural areas and to take steps to adjust agriculture, industry, and commerce, we can only strive to engage in cooperative national economic construction.

IV.

Finally, China's cooperative movement is a movement to create sound units of local self-government. Local self-government takes the complete security of the people's lives as a prerequisite, and the stability of the people's lives can only be guaranteed by the widespread development of cooperative enterprises. The Premier, in the law on the commencement of local self-government, pointed out that the undertakings to be undertaken by local self-government organizations include agricultural cooperation, industrial cooperation, trade cooperation, banking cooperation, and insurance cooperation, in addition to six items such as clearing household registration and establishing institutions. Cooperative enterprises are to follow the various cooperatives suggested by the Premier to establish a collective social life center. As a result of this development, it will surely succeed in becoming a central overall social organization. From this, the establishment of a social organization centered on cooperatives will promote the soundness of the basic unit of local self-government, and the realization of a truly national, classless, and democratic politics will be assured.

The China of the Three Principles of the People does not adopt the capitalist system that is gradually being destroyed, does not recognize classes, opposes struggle, and does not have the unique organization of socialist countries. The entire nation promotes the truth, goodness, and beauty of "life"; at the same time, it should coordinate the entire process of production and consumption.

Therefore, China's cooperative movement cannot blindly copy imported forms, but should, as mentioned above, under the basic principles of the Three Principles of the People, according to the great goals of national economic independence, national economic construction, and the establishment of sound local self-government, adopt a regular and appropriate posture. At the same time, China's cooperative system should also organically and closely link producers and consumers according to the various missions borne by China's cooperative movement, follow the categories suggested by the Premier, and carry out a peaceful, balanced, and universal development to establish the political and economic social center of the Three Principles of the People, and further create a fair, equal, fraternal world of great harmony, and build an unparalleled happy "Eden" for the whole world and all mankind.

The Film Industry Under the Control of Financial Capital

— Sha Tuo

Overview of the Film Industry in Various Countries by Sha Tuo

Film is the darling of the modern era, and the film industry has become one of the most important industries in the modern era. According to statistics from the U.S. Department of Commerce, there were 87,299 movie theaters worldwide last year, including 15,378 in the United States, 5,070 in the United Kingdom, 4,782 in Germany, 4,221 in Italy, 4,000 in France, 1,634 in Japan, and 1,833 in Czechoslovakia.

In terms of film production, the United States is, of course, the number one. On average, it can produce 700 popular films each year. The United Kingdom can produce 190 films a year, and Germany and France can each produce more than 100 films a year. Although the number of movie theaters in Japan is not as high as in the Czech Republic, the number of films produced each year is more than 400, second only to the United States, which cannot be considered a contradictory phenomenon.

Countries with thousands of movie theaters can only produce about 100 films each year, which is certainly not enough. Therefore, with the exception of the United States and Japan, movie theaters in other countries almost always show foreign films as well. The films produced in Japan are only enough for self-sufficiency and cannot be exported. The United States is certainly the most dominant force in the world film industry. Almost 70% to 80% of the films shown around the world are American films. Therefore, there is no country that does not feel the pressure of American films. As for China, it goes without saying. Just look at the first-class movie theaters in the country, how many of them are not using Hollywood beauties as a selling point!

The Financial Capitalization of the Film Industry

Although China's film industry has shown some vitality in recent years, it is still lagging behind in both quality and quantity. In terms of quantity, the annual film production is probably less than 50 films. In terms of quality, I wonder how many good films there are each year. Japanese films, although proud in terms of quantity, are mostly of poor quality. This is because film in Europe and the United States has become a large enterprise, with the assistance of financial capitalists. In China, the capital interest rate is at least one cent or more. Ordinary industries cannot afford this high-interest capital, let alone the emerging and immature film industry. We can see that the American film industry, although it only began to develop after the European War, has made rapid progress in the past 20 years. This is entirely due to the development of American financial capital after the European War, and the film industry has also become financially capitalized. The current investment in the film industry in the United States is more than 2 billion U.S. dollars. The cost of film production alone is 150 million U.S. dollars each year.

In addition to the United States, the film industries in the United Kingdom and Germany also have considerable financial capital power as a backing. In other countries, the degree of integration between the film industry and financial capital is very shallow.

The Absorption of Fixed Capital

The method of the film industry absorbing fixed capital is similar to that of general industries. In the United States, investment banks and trust companies are generally used to issue stocks or corporate bonds, and then they are publicly auctioned on the stock exchange. The bonds of the British film industry are mostly long-term, usually around 10 years. The film industries of France and Germany rarely issue their own bonds, and their funds mostly rely on bank supply. Therefore, the power to produce films is also in the hands of financial capitalists. Everyone knows that the boss of the German Ufa company is a arms dealer, so the films it produces are based on the principle of promoting militarism and advertising the sale of arms.

As for the production funds, they have a liquid nature and a short recovery period, so there is no need to issue bonds. For example, in the United States, the cost of making a film sometimes reaches 2 or 3 million yuan. This kind of funding must rely on banks. The American film production year starts in July each year. Around May or June, the film industry giants have to personally set out to negotiate loans with banks. However, banks are only willing to provide funds to film production companies, and are mostly unwilling to invest in individual producers. Therefore, individual producers mostly promote films to companies that sell films.

Most French films are personal works, and it is difficult to obtain financial assistance in their own country. In recent years, it has been invaded by American capital. American film companies often provide funds to outstanding French producers, and their works are sold in France and imported into the United States. This can be said to be a process of internationalization of the film industry.

After the National Socialist Party took power in Germany, it set up a propaganda department to control the film industry. On the one hand, it restricted the import of foreign films, and on the other hand, it promoted domestic films. The official Deutsche Bank has a huge investment in the Ufa film company every year. At the same time, there is a film industry credit bank that specializes in providing capital to individual producers.

Methods of American Banks Investing in the Film Industry

American banks or trust companies invest in production companies, usually on a per-film basis. Each film's loan must be contracted separately, so it can be called a fractional investment. When a film company wants to borrow money from a bank, it must first submit the following documents to the bank authorities: (1) the story of the film, (2) the cast, (3) the production budget, and (4) the financial report. As a result of the bank's review, if it believes that the story and the cast are perfectly matched, the work has the hope of success, and the production budget is indeed reliable, then it can order the loan. However, loans are paid as needed, just like current deposits. After the loan, the production company must submit a detailed production report every week, subject to bank supervision. If the bank believes that it does not conform to the pre-determined production procedure, it can stop paying the loan. Because of this, most American films can be released within the predetermined period.

Once the producer completes the negative film (the developed film, called negative film, its light and dark black and white are opposite to the captured object), it must be handed over to the bank for safekeeping as collateral for the loan. If the company that sells the film wants to reprint the positive film (PositireFilm is printed from the negative film, that is, the film shot on the screen), it can ask the bank to reprint it. However, the film sales company is responsible to the bank for handing over all the income from the new film to the bank for distribution. After receiving it, the bank first recovers the loan, and the surplus is handed over to the production company and the film sales company. After the bank recovers the loan, it can return the soft film.

The loan period is not fixed, and is generally based on the period of completion of the film. It is as early as three months and as late as six months. Loan interest is mostly deducted in advance from the loan.

Methods of the German Government Supporting the Film Industry

The method of German banks investing in production companies is roughly the same as that of the United States. Because the United States is an advanced country in the film industry, its investment methods and established rules are sufficient for other countries to emulate. However, German banks only lend 70% of the production cost per film to production companies, and the remaining 30% must be planned by the production company itself. This is afraid that the production company will rely on loans to install coarsely.

Germany has a film industry credit bank run jointly by the government and merchants, which can be said to be the only film industry bank in the world. This bank is the general organ of the National Socialist Party government that controls the national film industry. This bank has 30 million marks of government shares, directors appointed by the government, and directors appointed by the banking community. It is especially noteworthy that this bank is not only attended by important figures from the government and business circles, but also includes all industrial and commercial figures related to the film industry. For example, the film manufacturing company, sound film equipment experts, photography associations, and movie theaters all send representatives to be directors of this bank. Therefore, this bank has considerable supervision over the capital and technical aspects of the film industry. Only in this way can it implement the propaganda policy of the National Socialist Party.

The investment direction of this bank is all in individual producers. For example, if a famous expedition team wants to produce an adventure film and publicize the National Socialist Party's foreign policy, it can request a loan from this bank, and the bank can also send experts to guide it. In recent years, the achievements of German personal film production have been very satisfactory, which can be said to be entirely due to this bank.

The Development Path of China's Film Industry

China's film industry has indeed made progress in recent years, but compared with foreign films, both quality and quantity are still immature. The reason for this is that capital is lacking. Because of the lack of capital, the investment in personnel, equipment, and various aspects is inevitably simple and crude, and the production is of poor quality. What is even more pitiful is that even the crude and poorly made films that can be seen are only a few each year. Therefore, foreign films are imported in a steady stream. The economic loss goes without saying, and the impact on our spirit is great. Films from capitalist countries either promote the power of imperialism or advocate pornographic culture, and cannot be our spiritual food. Therefore, we should now learn from Germany and Japan, restrict the import of foreign films, and strive for film self-sufficiency. The government and the banking community should jointly assist domestic film companies. In this way, we can supervise the film industry and promote the rationalization of its film production methods and the scientificization of its management methods. If film production companies want to obtain capital assistance, they must also eliminate accumulated malpractices and strive for openness, and operate in a scientific manner. In terms of personnel and finance, everything must be open to the public, abandon the infighting between colleagues, and jointly build Chinese-based film art.

Correction Letter from Tianjin Beiyang Yarn Factory

To the editor: After reading the article titled "The Textile Industry in North China Under Japanese Control" in the Economic Supplement of your newspaper on July 20, I will not comment on whether the news about the various textile factories in Tianjin is completely reliable, but regarding the statement in your article that our factory was acquired by Japanese capital in June, this does not conform to the facts, and I hope you will correct it to avoid confusion. Our factory was originally leased and operated by Gongji, and it has suffered heavy losses in recent years, so it was transferred to Chengfu Trust Company for operation. All transfer and receiving procedures were completed on May 21, and it was published in the newspaper. Our company, for the livelihood of the workers, started operations on June 1. On the one hand, it actively reorganized, and it has been going smoothly for two months. On the other hand, it plans to thoroughly improve the original 25,000 spindles and expand it to more than 37,000 spindles. The drawings and plans have been largely finalized. This news has also been published in major newspapers in Tianjin, and I believe the editor has also seen it. Your newspaper has always been known for its fair and upright views and accurate news at home and abroad. Now, without careful investigation, it publishes this inaccurate text, which is a pity for your newspaper. I dare not speculate that the drafter has ulterior motives. In the future, regarding the news of the yarn factory, it is best to inquire in detail from the Cotton Industry Control Committee of the government agency or the Chinese Yarn Factory Federation of the commercial group, and do not engage in anti-propaganda for the national factory. I am very fortunate. Furthermore, the Chinese textile industry has been on the verge of danger in recent years due to various reasons. If the Chinese people and the government do not work together to save it, the national industry and the people's livelihood will be unimaginable. I hope you will take this into consideration. Chengfu Management Beiyang Commercial First Textile Factory. July 24.

Editor's note: In the article "The Textile Industry in North China Under Japanese Control" published in this supplement on July 20, regarding the Beiyang Yarn Factory, the editor added an annotation when sending the manuscript, just to cast doubt and verify the facts, which I think is what the readers have seen. After receiving the letter from the Beiyang Factory, I immediately inquired from the reply from the writer Sen Yu, only to know that the source of this news was "seen in the Shanghai China Daily on June 22, and also in the talks of the leaders of the yarn industry published in the Shanghai Daily Evening News on July 5 and 6, and in the Central News Agency Beiping telegram in the Current Affairs News on July 12, and in the Beiping special telegram in the China Daily on July 13. Since I saw the Tianjin telegram from your newspaper, the manuscript has been sent out, and it is too late to revise it. The person (the writer calls himself) deeply hopes that what was transmitted by the previous newspapers is not true, so that the national industry can retain a glimmer of hope, which is what we urgently hope for," and so on. Since it is based on newspaper reports, and the Beiyang Yarn Factory only corrected it after this article was published, it can be seen that it is not "ulterior motives" and "anti-propaganda."

Securities: Public Debt Last Week, Abruptly Turned Downstream After Delivery

Last week, from July 27 to August 1, the Huashang Securities Exchange was for the delivery of futures for July and the listing of futures for September. After another round of sharp rise in the market situation, it gradually turned downstream. The reason is that the market's rising wind was too strong. Once the floating long positions were released, it immediately caused fluctuations. Last week, only the August futures were traded on Monday. People's minds were extremely firm, and it rose another 8 jiao to 1 yuan 2 jiao. With the Guangdong affairs settled, this is a natural phenomenon. On Tuesday, the filming of the September futures began. The opening price was particularly attractive. Buyers were eager, fearing to fall behind. Category A even saw a high price of 70 yuan. Compared with the highest price of 71 yuan including interest in July, it exceeded a huge amount of 2 yuan, which was really too high. Therefore, there was no rumor in the decisive settlement, and the return wind had risen, and it suddenly returned more than half a yuan. However, it still rose by 1 jiao to 1 yuan or so. Wednesday was the delivery of July futures, and the market was closed. On Thursday, news from Guizhou Province poured in, and the floating long positions were uncertain. The falling wind immediately rose, falling by 8 jiao to 1 yuan 4 jiao. However, the market price was too high, and a slight loss could not stop the short side's selling. Although it was relatively stable on Friday, the falling wind was still huge on Saturday, falling another 1 yuan. Categories E, D, and C have all returned to the 60 yuan mark, and most of them have returned from the highest price by more than 2 yuan to more than 3 yuan. Sugar Market: Slight Decrease in Local Sugar Inventory

High Grade Refined Sugar Jumps Up by One Yuan

Yesterday, in the Sugar Exchange market, varieties such as Grade 24 granulated white sugar and Dong White showed little fluctuation. However, domestic sugar continued to trend upward. The quotation boards showed Guangdong and Chaozhou brokers offering 1,300 bales of Hainan Red at a high of 13.45 yuan, followed by 13.30 to 13.10 yuan, an increase of 30 to 40 cents. De Faxiang offered about 1,300 bales of mixed brand raw cotton sugar at a price of 14.85 yuan. Shengji Red was offered at 15.40 yuan for 40 bales, Huaguang Red at 15.20 yuan for 31 bales, and Changsheng Tongfa Red a total of 111 bales at 15.00 yuan, with ordinary sugar at 14.50 yuan for 34 bales. Newly arrived cotton refined Zheng Tiqing was offered at 14.00 yuan for 50 bales, up one yuan. Existing stock of refined Tiqing was offered at 13.00 yuan for over a hundred bales.

Seafood: Squid Shortage Leads to Price Increase

(Squid) Currently, the inventory in the city is scarce across all shops, especially for the box-packed squid, which is even more in short supply. Recently, Sichuan brokers have been actively purchasing. According to a telegram from Hakodate, over a hundred packages have already been shipped. However, due to supply shortages and price increases in the producing area, the cost of the goods in transit is estimated to be 88 or 89 yuan. Local merchants who received the news earlier have already been pre-selling to customers, with asking prices around 90 yuan, waiting for the goods to arrive and quickly resell them. Second-grade squid for Zhou is selling for 83 yuan for old stock, 84 yuan for cold storage stock, and 85 yuan for improved stock (high-quality box-packed squid). The inventory of American-produced Golden Mountain canned squid is also dwindling, with current transactions around 80 yuan.

80,000 Spectators Attend the Second Day of the World Games; Owens Sets World Record in 100m; Owens Runs 10.2 Seconds in Second Round, 10.3 Seconds in Preliminary Round; Yesterday, Chinese Athletes Fail to Qualify in All Four Preliminary Events; New World Record Also Set in Women's Javelin Preliminary Round

(Berlin) The 11th Olympic Games opened today with participants from 50 countries. (Dispatch from Central News Agency Special Correspondent on the 1st) The United States, which dominated the sprint events at the Los Angeles Olympics four years ago, seems likely to maintain its authority at this year's Olympics. Jesse Owens clocked an astonishing 10.3 seconds in the 100m preliminary round, equalling the 1932 record of the bespectacled intellectual runner Tolan of Michigan. Owens' time was the best of today's preliminary rounds. In the second round, Owens further set a new world record with 10.2 seconds, witnessed by 80,000 spectators. (Reuters dispatch on the 2nd)

(Berlin) At 10:30 AM on the 2nd, the men's 100m preliminary rounds were held at the stadium, divided into 12 groups, with the top two from each group qualifying. Chinese athlete Zhuang Jincheng got off to a slightly slow start in the fifth group, falling behind by five meters and failing to qualify. Cheng Jinguan, in the eighth group, fought bravely but finished fourth, six meters behind and failing to qualify. Liu Changchun had a good start in the eleventh group, running second until 30 meters, but then ran out of steam and failed to qualify by six meters. Simultaneously, the men's high jump preliminary round started at 1.70 meters, rising to 1.80 meters. Chinese athlete Wu Bi'xian cleared both heights, but failed to clear 1.85 meters on all three attempts, touching the bar on the third attempt and being eliminated. Also, the men's shot put preliminary round was held at the same location at 11:00 AM, where Chinese athlete Chen Baoqiu also failed to qualify. (Dispatch from Central News Agency Special Correspondent on the 2nd)

(Berlin) China was unlucky today, with no athletes qualifying in four different preliminary events. Those eliminated were Zhuang Jincheng and Cheng Jinguan in the 100m, Wu Bi'xian in the high jump, and Chen Baoqiu in the shot put. Liu Changchun did not participate. Zhuang Jincheng participated in the fifth group of the preliminary round and had a good start, taking the lead until halfway, but gradually fell behind and finished fourth. The first place in this group was McFeigh of Canada, with a time of 10.8 seconds. Cheng Jinguan also had a good start in the eighth group preliminary round, but also finished fourth. The first place in this group was Buschmeyer of Germany, with a time of 10.7 seconds. (Reuters dispatch on the 2nd)

Central News Agency Special Correspondent Berlin, 2nd. The 800m preliminary round of the World Games was held at 4:00 PM on the 2nd, divided into six groups. In the third group, Chinese athlete Jia Yunren bravely surged forward after the start. He was in fourth place after the first lap, but then gradually ran out of strength, finishing sixth, 60 meters behind.

Grand Opening of the Olympic Games; US Athletes Do Not Salute the Podium

German Athlete Representative Takes Oath

At that time, the cannons fired in unison, and 1,000 homing pigeons were released simultaneously. The Olympic torch was then carried into the stadium by German athletes, and the Olympic flame was lit. This flame will continue to burn until the closing day of the Games on August 16th. After the opening ceremony, Louis, the winner of the marathon at the first Games, presented an "olive branch," symbolizing peace, to Chancellor Hitler. The audience then stood up and cheered, and the orchestra played a new Olympic piece composed by the famous German composer Strauss. Then, Ismer, a German athlete who had won a championship at the previous Games, led the team leaders from each country in taking the oath. Ismer stood in the middle, with the team leaders from each country standing around him in a semicircle. The ceremony was very solemn. The athletes of each country then left the stadium in formation, and the audience cheered to send them off.

Berlin, Reuters, 2nd. Yesterday, the World Games were declared open by Chancellor Hitler with a simple speech, saying "I now declare the 11th Olympic Games open." Over ten thousand participants cheered before Hitler, and the 5,000 athletes from 52 countries passed by, saluting with the Nazi Party salute or other salutes. Thirty thousand homing pigeons were released, so that they could spread the news of the opening of the Games all over the earth. At the same time, the crowd sang the national anthem and the Horst Wessel song. The orchestra, led by the famous composer Strauss, played the Olympic song. At this time, a German athlete carried the torch from Greece to Hitler's platform and lit the Olympic flame. This flame will be extinguished only after the closing ceremony. When the Chinese team passed the podium, they received great cheers and did not perform the Nazi salute, but only removed their hats and placed them on their chests. When the American team passed in front of the podium, they suddenly received some boos, because the American team did not salute. (American rules do not allow the flag to be lowered, and some of the athletes in the team did not remove their headscarves.)

Havas, Berlin, 1st. The opening ceremony of the 11th Olympic Games was held this afternoon at 4:00 PM, with unprecedented grandeur and solemnity. From early morning, spectators had been entering the stadium one after another, waiting quietly. By the time of the opening, the stadium and surrounding streets were packed with people, totaling no less than 250,000. The Hindenburg zeppelin flew in the sky, circling the stadium several times, and the spectators cheered when they saw it. German Chancellor Hitler arrived at the venue at 3:30 PM, wearing a yellow uniform, with an Iron Cross on his chest and a swastika armband on his left arm. When he entered the stadium, the crowd stood up and sang the national anthem "Deutschland über alles", and all raised their arms in the Nazi salute. Then, a German girl presented the Chancellor with a bouquet of flowers. Shortly after, the national flag of the Chancellor and the five-ring flag of the Olympic Games were hoisted on either side of the podium. At this time, members of the Storm Troopers sang the national anthem in unison, and then the Olympic bell on the high tower rang out, and the flags of the 52 nations slowly rose to the top of the flagpoles and fluttered in the sky.

Louis Leads the International Parade

The athletes of each country then formed a team and entered the stadium, parading around the stadium once. The leader was Louis, a Greek who won the marathon at the first Olympic Games in 1896. He was 65 years old, dressed in ancient Greek costume, full of spirit, and marched forward. The audience cheered wildly. After Louis were the athletes of the Greek team, because the Olympic Games originated in Greece. The athletes of other countries marched in order according to the first letter of their country's name, and the last was the German athletes, as Germany was the host of the Games and should be at the rear. When the German athletes entered the stadium, the audience sang the national anthem again to welcome them.

Hitler Announces the Opening of the Games

After the parade, the athletes of each country lined up in the center of the stadium, standing quietly. Each team had a leader holding the national flag, standing in the front row, facing the podium. A small podium was set up in the center of the stadium. First, Lewald, Chairman of the German Committee of the Olympic Games, took the stage to speak, paying tribute to Baron Pierre de Coubertin of France, the founder of the modern Olympic Games. After his speech, Chancellor Hitler officially announced the opening of the Games.

Light Rain Does Not Reduce Enthusiasm

National Maritime News Agency, Berlin, August 1st. 100,000 spectators had already gathered in the stadium before the scheduled opening time, in a fervent mood, waiting for this grand opening ceremony. Although it was drizzling, the enthusiasm of the spectators was not diminished. The only addition to the stadium was countless umbrellas. The "Hindenburg Men's Airship" appeared in the sky over the stadium, slowly approaching, like a large crow, and the crowds around the stadium were all able to see it clearly.

"I Awaken the Youth of the World"

At exactly 4:00 PM, German Chancellor Hitler, Count de La Tour, Dr. Lewald, and members of the Olympic Committee, all dressed in morning dress and wearing full chains, entered from the west entrance of the stadium, one after another. As the 100,000 spectators stood up to salute, the orchestra immediately played the German national anthem. Hitler then proceeded to the front of the stage and took his seat. At that moment, the drizzle stopped and the weather cleared up again. Umbrellas were no longer seen in the stadium until the end of the ceremony.

The Olympic bell, hanging high on a 70-meter-high monument tower, rang loudly at this time, announcing its mission, saying "I awaken the youth of the world." As the cannons fired, the flags of the 52 nations rose one after another around the stadium, fluttering in the wind.

Athletes From All Nations Enter the Stadium in Single File

At this time, those whom the spectators had traveled thousands of miles to see were now present: the athletes from all nations entering the stadium in single file, passing the Chancellor's observation platform, circling the track once, and then regrouping in the center of the stadium.

Each team was led by an adjutant holding a white board with the name of the country written in German. Following this white board was the flag bearer of that country, and the coaches and managers of the team were arranged behind them. Finally came the athletes. The stadium was dazzling, because the uniforms worn by the athletes of each country were specially made and even more pleasing to the eye.

Each Team Salutes in Unique Ways

The salute of each team to Hitler was unique. No two of the 51 teams were the same.

The first team to enter the stadium was the Greek team, and the last was the German team. The athletes from the remaining countries were arranged according to the German alphabet of their country's name. Therefore, the Egyptian team (Egyptians) was the first, because Egypt in German is (Aegypten).

The Egyptian team saluted Chancellor Hitler with a raised hand, but the Argentine team turned to the right as a whole. The Austrian team lowered their flag to the ground, and the Belgians marched in goose step. The South African team removed their hats as a salute. As for the Swiss team, they had a special idea. The flag bearer threw the flag into the air and then caught it with his hand, doing so several times. The teams from Castile and Haiti saluted with shouts, but since each team had only one person, there was no one to echo the shout except for the flag bearer. When the French team entered the stadium, the entire stadium was silent. When the team's flag bearer passed in front of Hitler's observation platform, he lowered the tricolor flag almost to the ground, and all the team members gave the Olympic salute. Apart from the Austrian team, the French team was the most popular with the audience.

The Olympic Games Are Declared Open

After each team was in place, Dr. Lewald, in a brief speech, described the meaning of the Olympics. After this speech, Hitler stood up and said, "I declare the Olympic Games open." At that time, the applause was thunderous, and the people cheered. Amidst this enthusiasm, 3,000 homing pigeons were released at the same time. Many of them circled the stadium, admiring the athletes, and then flew off. Finally, the last bearer of the World Games torch, dressed entirely in white, walked slowly down the stone steps, across the stadium, holding the torch. The torch relay of thousands of miles had come to an end.

120,000 Homing Pigeons Released

On the opening day of the World Games, a total of 110,000 homing pigeons were released, with the aim of spreading the news of the opening of the World Games to all countries in Europe, and to compete for the fastest time. Many of these homing pigeons came from various parts of Germany, and also from Sweden, Denmark, Poland, Czechoslovakia, Hungary, Greece, Italy, and Austria. They have been released since 5:00 AM this morning, including many that have flown over 1,500 kilometers. The Olympic Committee has prizes for the winners.

National Maritime News Agency, Berlin, August 2nd. The German women's javelin team has entered the final round this afternoon. German Frau Fiehe achieved the highest score of 44.6 化 meters. Nobles from Various Countries Visit the German Chancellor

Havas, Berlin, 1st. German Crown Prince Wilhelm, Greek Crown Prince Paul, and Swedish Prince Gustav Adolf have arrived here one after another to attend the Olympic Games. They visited German Chancellor Hitler today and had a brief conversation.

The International Committee Receives Hitler; Mayor of Athens Sends Congratulatory Telegram

Havas, Berlin, 1st. The International Olympic Committee held a meeting today to receive Chancellor Hitler. The Chairman, Count Baillet Latour of Belgium, stood up to give a speech, saying that the Chancellor was very interested in the Games and that the International Committee was extremely grateful. Hitler replied that he was very pleased that the International Committee had chosen Berlin as the venue for this year's Games, and that Germany was willing to use the spirit of the Olympic Games to promote close relations between nations and enrich them.

National News Agency, Berlin, August 1st. Hitler received a congratulatory telegram from the Mayor of Athens today. The original text is as follows: "As the World Games torch is passed to the Berlin stadium, I would like to sincerely congratulate you and the German people on realizing this grand plan."

Various Aspects of the Olympic Games (3)

— Jiang Huaiqing

(3) Members

To date, the International Olympic Committee (the administrative body of the Olympics) has 55 member nations. They are listed below in alphabetical order by the first letter of their English names: Afghanistan, Argentina, Australia, Austria, Belgium, Brazil, Bulgaria, Canada, Chile, China, Colombia, Cuba, Czechoslovakia, Denmark, Uganda, Egypt, Estonia, Finland, France, Germany, Great Britain, Greece, Haiti, Netherlands, Honduras, Hungary, India, Irish Free State, Iceland, Italy, Japan, Latvia, Lithuania, Luxembourg, Malta, Mexico, Monaco, New Zealand, Norway, Panama, Peru, Philippines, Poland, Portugal, Rhodesia, Romania, Russia, South Africa, Spain, Sweden, Switzerland, Turkey, Uruguay, United States, Yugoslavia.

(4) The First Games

Looking back at the first revived Olympic Games held in Athens, the capital of Greece, in 1896, everything was beyond the imagination of later generations. However, for an era forty years ago, such a grand scale was truly unexpected. The venue for the first meeting was a long and magnificent building, standing at the foot of Mount Hymettos and extending to the left bank of the River Ilisos. This ancient sports ground, recorded in history books, was able to reappear in the modern world. This sports ground was the first of its kind in modern Europe to be completed, funded solely by a patriotic Greek, Averoff. It is now the venue for the first Olympic Games. The forty-eight rows of marble grandstands added to its brilliance and grandeur, making it a sight to behold.

A total of thirty-four nations were invited to participate, but in reality, only twelve nations participated in the competition. There were only twelve events, and most of them were traditional Greek ancient programs. The people of Athens were in a state of excitement, and the whole city was decorated in splendor. The most exciting event was the marathon, a pure essence of ancient Greek national sport. The winner was greatly honored. King George I, accompanied by the Crown Prince, watched at the finish line and did not hesitate to shake hands with the marathon winner, Luis. His attendants also stepped forward to embrace Luis. At this time, Luis was no less than a triumphant general of ancient times.

German Discus Champion, Rabaut

Educational News

Over Twenty Cultural Organizations to Hold Farewell Party for Students Studying Abroad; 4:00 PM on the 16th in the City Hall Auditorium; Mayor Wu to Preside and Tang Shaoyi to Give Speech

The farewell party for students studying abroad, initiated by the World Student Association and the Municipal Education Bureau, held a preparatory meeting yesterday at 5:00 PM at the International Hotel, gathering various organizations. It was decided to hold the event at 4:00 PM on the afternoon of the 16th of this month in the City Hall Auditorium. Details are as follows:

Attending Representatives: Including Zhu Shaoping and Wu Deyin from the World Student Association; Shi Weicong from the Municipal Education Bureau; Mu Ouchu and Guo Bingwen from the Local Association; Zou Bingwen; Wang Xiaolai from the Municipal Chamber of Commerce; Huang Zhaoxiong from the Municipal Education Association; Shi She from the Vocational Education Society; Kuang Yaokun from the International Affairs Research Association; Wu Zijing from the German-Austrian Alumni Association; Hu Duanxing from Jiaotong University; Du Zuozhou from Jinan University; Hu Qibing from Guanghua University; Gu Yinming from Nanyang Middle School; Xu Wanshan from Qixiu Girls' Middle School; Ma Chonggan from Shen Bao; Hu Shuyi from Xinwen Bao; Zhu Yixin from Min Bao; Huang Zhechong from Zhonghua Daily; Zhu Shaoping from China Review; Gu Futang from Dalu Bao; Huang Jingwan from Commercial Press; Wang Shilin from Zhonghua; and Shen Enqi from Shijie, totaling over thirty representatives from over twenty organizations.

Foreign Faculty Members and Monthly Salaries in National Higher Education

The Ministry of Education has recently compiled statistics on foreign faculty and staff members and monthly salaries in national colleges and universities (including universities, independent colleges, and vocational schools). An overview is extracted below:

(1) "University Aspect": There are 34 national, provincial, and private universities in the country that employ foreign faculty and staff. The number of employed personnel is 497. By position, there are 444 teachers and 53 staff members. The total monthly salary is 128,837 yuan (24,197 yuan for teachers and 14,640 yuan for staff). By category, 13 national universities have a monthly salary of 32,795 yuan for faculty and staff, 5 provincial universities have 1,782 yuan, and 16 private universities have 94,260 yuan. The highest monthly salary for teachers is 1,500 yuan at Aurora University, and the lowest is 50 yuan at Zhejiang University (this refers to full-time employees). The highest monthly salary for staff is 1,000 yuan at Tongji University, and the lowest is 80 yuan at Aurora University (full-time).

(2) "College Aspect": A total of 18 national, provincial, and private independent colleges in the country employ foreign faculty and staff. The number of employed personnel is 177. By position, there are 125 teachers and 52 staff members. The total monthly salary is 32,418 yuan (23,160 yuan for teachers and 9,258 yuan for staff). By category, the monthly salary for faculty and staff is 9,876 yuan for 3 national independent colleges, 1,977 yuan for 4 provincial colleges, and 21,565 yuan for 11 private colleges. The highest monthly salary for teachers is 870 yuan at Peiyang Institute of Technology, and the lowest is 100 yuan at Tianjin Business College. The highest monthly salary for staff is 600 yuan at the Sino-French Institute of Technology, and the lowest is 150 yuan at Tianjin Business College (the lowest numbers refer to full-time employees).

(3) "Specialized School Aspect": There are 7 national, public, and private specialized schools in the country that employ foreign teachers. The number of employed personnel is 30. By position, there are 29 teachers and 1 staff member. The total monthly salary is 5,039 yuan (4,689 yuan for teachers and 250 yuan for staff). The highest monthly salary for teachers is 410 yuan at Beiping Taxation School, and the lowest is 50 yuan at Wuchang Wenhua Library and Preparatory School (full-time).
