Spring and Autumn

Counterproductive

— (Chen Liang)

On the road, there are already coolies who have "died of heatstroke," and the epidemic hospitals are also very "busy." The atmosphere is really heating up. "Fiery umbrellas rise high" and "the Red Emperor displays his power" are phrases that old newsmen can use. In this boiler-like situation, people who cannot afford the economic time to climb to the top of the mountain and lie on the beach have to form an inseparable bond with ice and fans.

Eating ice, fanning, going to roof gardens, going to swimming pools, people think are the only ways to relieve the heat. Therefore, ice, fans, gardens, water... are all regarded as kind and lovely cool places and cool things. Without these, there would be no way to spend the summer. But in fact, there are also those that are counterproductive. Look at the children on the streets scorched by the sun, covered in sweat, shouting "Shade, buy ice..." Why are their necks so red? Isn't a large piece of ice in their hands? But they are running and shouting because they are worried about the melting of the ice, and they feel even hotter from the effort of running and shouting.

This shows that: although the essence of ice is cool, those who sell coolness cannot enjoy it. In the shackles of life, even the things around oneself become a "burden" in the opposite direction.

Miss Ice Cream

— Hua Ling

At the "Dali Ice Cream Parlor" behind the three French parasol trees at the intersection, when Ice Cream was launched, a beautiful girl like a little bird came, with jet-black hair, dark eyes, and a curvy figure, between the glass-covered round tables. Like a butterfly, she fluttered around, serving the gentlemen-type customers in the whole room. She can speak fluent English, a few superficial French sentences, Mandarin with a three-point Hunan accent, and a few non-vulgar Cantonese sentences. Someone asked her what her surname was? She smiled playfully and said, "Ice Cream." So everyone called her "Miss Ice Cream."

It is said that this Miss Ice Cream was recruited through an advertisement in the old newspaper, with a contract for two months, and a monthly salary of forty yuan. At the same time, 5% of the total income of these two months is also paid as a bonus. According to estimates, she may be able to get about two yuan a day. In addition to the extra small account, she may get ten yuan a day. Because in the Dali Ice Cream Parlor. From morning to night, it is full of guests, because Miss Ice Cream is indeed too cute. A certain Dr. said that sitting in the Dali Ice Cream Parlor served by Miss Ice Cream can make you forget the high heat of more than 100 degrees on the street. So he goes to Dali at least three times a day and forgets the homework of the evening dance hall.

It is said that this Miss Ice Cream was born to a Guangdong father and a Changsha mother. She is currently a junior in the Department of Literature at a certain university in Beiping. This summer, she came to Shanghai for a trip with a friend, and temporarily filled the role of a daughter to entertain. Her family. Is very wealthy, so she plans to donate all the rewards she has received in these two months to several charitable organizations for expenses. Recently, she has been very interested in this kind of professional life. She said, "I may be able to get a lot of life experience in these two months. If I can get enough materials from the customers, perhaps, before the summer vacation next year, I will write a planned My Client."

Recently, there are often admirers who ask her for photos. She always charges a price of two yuan and gives a half-length photo of six and a half inches signed in English "A Promoter of Charity - Ice Cream." Because of the price of these two yuan, she also plans to donate all of it to charitable organizations. In addition, she has to receive one or twenty letters from strangers every day, some of which are teasing. When she receives these letters, she always says, "This is too superficial," and dismisses it with a smile.

Lotus

— Yi Mei

The lotus flower is noble and supreme, truly as Zhou Dunyi said: "It emerges from the mud yet remains unstained, it is washed by the clear ripples yet is not seductive, it stands tall and pure, its fragrance travels far and becomes more clear." Those who live in Shanghai are limited by their location and do not have a pond to plant lotuses, so they place one or two tile jars in the courtyard, with green leaves and red buds swaying between the sparse curtains. They feel that this is a kind of scenery. Comforting emotions is better than nothing, and it is appropriate.

The Six Yan Zhai Notes says: "Every year when the lotus first emerges from the water, before it reaches the edge of the leaves, it is often nipped by sudden rain. I came up with a new idea: cut lotus leaves and sew them into the shape of a helmet, called the lotus hat. Before the rain, I covered them all over, which was very helpful. I joked and sang: "If you want to spread your Lingbo steps, you must first prepare for the rain. The jade cover is deeply covering your forehead, and you are quietly hiding your fragrance. Don't rely on the tilted pearl cover, you should be the same as the jade sac inside. Pity yourself for being so small, waiting for the grace of light. If Master Lianxi knew, he would surely draw the owner of Six Yan Zhai as his confidant.

There is a secret to planting lotus: adding pig hair to the bottom can make the flowers flourish. Another way to tell whether the lotus will bloom is to look at the green veins on the leaf surface. If there are twenty-four, a flower will bloom. Also, if it does not bloom for a long time, it must be because of insufficient fertilizer. You can choose the deep green leaves and pick off a few stems to prevent them from absorbing too much nourishment, then the flowers will bloom faster.

In the past, Li Yu said: "The lotus is pleasing to the eye and the mouth. As for what is pleasing to the mouth, the lotus seeds and lotus roots are both placed on the table and mutually fragrant to the teeth." Gao Lian's Four Seasons Leisure Appreciation also said: "The taste of lotus seeds is best in the early morning. The water vapor floats at night, and it is just enough at this time. If the sun comes out and the dew dries, the freshness has gone by more than half. When staying overnight on the side of the Yue Wang Temple, there are the most lake lotuses. Slice a hundred rooms in the morning and eat them to your heart's content. Lotus root is best when it has been drained of water, and the green color is the most beautiful." With such a blessing, I don't envy the gods.

Sun Shushi and Lan Wei said that when they were young, they once traveled to Yuyuan Garden to watch Siamese lotuses. In those years, many famous people wrote poems and sang in harmony, and the good works were like a forest. The elegant story has been handed down, and even today there are those who can tell it. Since my family moved to the south of the city, Yuyuan Garden is close at hand. Unfortunately, the garden has been turned into public property and is not allowed to enter. I don't know if the jade fragrance and flower shadows still present auspicious signs or not.

Cool Breeze Cave

— Shang Shi

The Cool Breeze Cave of Stone Peng Mountain in Zhuji is the only cool and refreshing place during the sweltering summer. It is about twenty miles from the city, filled with crisscrossing and disorderly rocks with very few gaps. The cave is located halfway up the mountain, and beside it is a solitary temple, desolate and bleak. After taking a few steps, one arrives at the Cool Breeze Cave. The cave entrance is not wide, about three feet in diameter, so one must stoop to enter. Gradually, it becomes higher, and after more than ten feet, the rocks rise up, higher than the entrance, allowing one to stand upright. However, within, the yin wind howls angrily, and the cold air is oppressive. After two or three feet, many dare not go further. The rocks are jagged, with many side caves, all dark and without light. The cave is also narrow, requiring crawling. One must have a light and hold a rope. Because the cave is deep and winding, one end of the rope must be tied outside the cave, and the other end held while proceeding, releasing it as one goes. When exiting the cave, one can return by following the rope, avoiding the suffering of getting lost. Because the cave is yin and cold, one can freeze food inside even during the hottest days. If one is sweating profusely while climbing the mountain, upon reaching the cave, one will immediately feel the cold air penetrating the heart, requiring a lined jacket. The coolness is truly evident. Cold air often spills out of the cave, appearing as a misty smoke when viewed from afar. Near the rocky cliffs, the cave is dripping wet, even more refreshing. Locals say the cave is extremely deep, leading directly to the Qiantang River; however, no one has ever been able to reach its end, so the truth of this cannot be verified. There are many local legends about the cave; some say that thirty-six immortals once played the xiao and flute near the cave; others say that the cave was formed by the disorderly rocks from King Qian Chu’s whipping of the mountain. These are all folk tales and cannot be relied upon.

—

Even if the inside of a watermelon is a cool and refreshing world, what a pity for the knife that cuts it!

The Phoenixes Switch Nests

— Written by Zhang Henshui

Chapter 4: Sight and Sound are Uncertain, Floating and Sinking; Life and Death Can Be Entrusted, Generously Sending Elegies

Although the snow-white rice was served in a large bowl, it did not arouse his appetite. He had no choice but to sit down, pick up his chopsticks, and first select a small pinch of white rice, putting it in his mouth to chew. Old Mrs. Tong sat at the head of the table, just about to pick up her chopsticks and bowl, when she saw his listless appearance, so she asked: "Why can't you eat?" Guoqi smiled: "This afternoon, I ate some snacks at school. Now that it's time to eat, I don't feel like eating." Old Mrs. Zhang said: "If you can't eat, then don't eat." Guoqi said: "I just want to eat tea-soaked rice with some pickles." Old Mrs. Zhang said: "You are using your mind a lot these days, but you can't eat too much, as that easily leads to food stagnation." Guoqi couldn't help but be touched by this. His mother's thoughtfulness was indeed comprehensive. So he pushed away half a bowl of rice and soaked the remaining rice thoroughly with tofu soup, then slurped it down. After the meal, Old Mrs. Zhang said: "I told you not to eat, but you insisted on eating this large half-bowl. Don't go to the study to read right away, go out and play, or chat with friends." Guoqi naturally couldn't refuse his mother's words, but he was feeling very passive, so he put on his hat and went out, wandering around the nearby alleys. He didn't particularly pay attention, but his feet naturally led him to the alley near the Jiang family's residence. By this time, the sky was already dark, and the long, straight alley seemed even more gloomy. Although there were electric lights in this residential area, there was only one light for every few dozen households. That one electric light, on the electric pole, emitted a yellowish color, which seemed particularly desolate to those with worries. Just as he was walking slowly like this, feeling very uneasy, a large door opened beside him. Two women came out. The woman in front held a glass lantern, muttering: "We have to go to the main street again. Our young lady is sick again. Always bothering people." The woman behind said: "Look at the back building, it's open on three sides. On nights with a big moon, she opens the windows to admire the moon. Letting the cool breeze blow all night, how could she not get sick?" The woman with the lantern said: "Where did she catch a chill? She even went out this afternoon. I think girls get preoccupied when they grow up. She's suffering from lovesickness." As they spoke, the two women walked away. The large door was half-closed, revealing a sliver of light. Guoqi looked closely and saw that it was indeed the Jiang family's residence. Because he passed through the nearby area every day, going through dozens of alleys, he had occasionally walked through this place before. Once, he had seen Jiang Menglan getting out of a rickshaw here. (55)

Special Feature

Ice Cream Factory Sketch

— Yu Qing

It's hot! It's that time of year again when ice cream hits the market. Indeed, it seems that for Shanghainese people who are so particular about food, they only have ice cream to rely on to get through the summer. So ice cream has become the only summer treat for the privileged class. However, the workers who make ice cream don't get to taste it, even though they sweat while they work.

We walked past Linban Road and entered the ×× Ice Cream Factory. We were greeted by a young man in a Western suit. We signed our names in the visitor's registration book and began the tour.

We climbed up to the fourth floor, which was the mixing room—where the raw materials for ice cream are blended. However, when we visited, we didn't see anyone mixing ingredients, perhaps because they had already stopped? Only two or three workers were cleaning up. We just listened to the report from our host, like listening to a teacher explain the principles in a science class, giving us a report on the ingredients and procedures for mixing ice cream. There was also a machine for making artificial butter, and we only saw waxy yellow things that looked like inferior soap bars constantly rolling out.

We went back downstairs, passed the laboratory, and then went to the freezing room, where the mixture from the mixing room is sent to be frozen. This is where the ice cream sold on the market is made. All the packing is done by female workers, and we saw them constantly packing. According to our host, there are four freezers in the freezing room, and each freezer can make ten gallons of ice cream in fifteen minutes. Each gallon can be packed into about six dozen paper packages. He also said: "We produce at least one thousand gallons a day." From this, we can imagine the eating power and consumption level of the people in the metropolis.

On the way back, the scorching sun beat down on our heads and backs, making us feel uncomfortably hot. As we passed a corner, we saw a rickshaw puller drinking tea from a roadside tea stand. Then, a contrasting scene of an exquisite ice cream parlor flashed into my mind.

We entered the house, covered in stinky sweat.

Xiaochun Kan

Summer Special

A Calm Mind is Naturally Cool

— (Baiguo)

Actually, what is this secret? Even women and children know it. But everyone is unwilling to follow it! That method is the saying that a calm mind is naturally cool. Except for those high officials who already have electric fans and ice soda. This is indeed a unique and economical way to cool off that suits the common people, so why don't people do it? In fact, one only needs to take a detached view of everything external. Why always be restless, just shortening your lifespan? Moreover, in the hot summer, if your mind is calm, the inside is cool, and the outside is also cool, isn't that good?

Escaping the Heat at a Waterside Pavilion

— Cai Xuanqing

Zhao Kui, the Song Dynasty Prime Minister, a native of Liyang County, was at the time an admonisher, impeaching him for being illiterate. Kui angrily resigned, and although an imperial edict was issued to appease him and keep him in office, he firmly refused to comply. He returned home and built two waterside pavilions, one in the north of the county and one in the south, several miles apart. He would escape the heat in the pavilions during the summer. He once composed a line: "The waterside pavilion is surrounded by vermilion railings on all four sides, and schools of fish play among the duckweed." The six dragons fear the heat and cannot travel, and the sea water boils away, revealing the Penglai Island. Lying asleep with a seven-foot white beard, his head pillowed on a branch of green agate. He only composed six lines before falling asleep, and his serving maid, Lianxiang, added the rest: "The Prime Minister still finds the fan too weak, and the travelers are still on the dusty road." Her phrasing was elegant and reminiscent of Zheng Jia's poetry maid. I recall that when I was in the army for more than ten years, marching in the intense heat was the most difficult thing. I sought the shade of a wretched tree to rest for a moment, but it was not to be found. I happened to see layers of clouds blocking the sun, and I immediately felt a moment of coolness, and I composed a line, "The fiery parasol in the sky burns fiercely, and the travelers on the dusty road suffer the most. How can I always have thick clouds blocking the sun, so that a cool shade can be spread everywhere to dispel the heat?"

Escaping the Heat in Keyan

— Sun Linchang

Keyan in Shaoxing is truly a cool and refreshing world. Hu Tianyou's "Collection of Shijian Mountain House" lists the stone quarries of Yue, praising the Seven Star Rock of Ke Xi, praising the artificial axe carvings for their strange shapes. If we enter Keyan in the summer, we have not only the cool stone chambers that caress the skin, but also the tall bamboos that shield the sunlight. And the several pools of blue water and the broken railings also stir up people's secluded emotions. However, there are also some questionable aspects, which lie in the dilapidated state of the buildings, the lack of cleanliness, and the scarcity of pavilions and courtyards where visitors can sit, lie down, and rest. The other day, a newspaper carried a report about a Shanghai travel agency promoting escaping the heat in Keyan; the stone colors, pool light, and gloomy coldness of Keyan can indeed attract summer tourists.

The umbrella-like sun hangs in the sky, and summer has quietly arrived in the world. The whole of Shanghai is melting.

The Road to Health

Record of the Appearance of Inferior Medicines

— Physician Wu Zhonglin, Graduate of Nantong Medical University

The Failure of "Transmembrane Sterilization" Drugs

Mr. Wang, who lives on Nanjing Road, contracted gonorrhea about two months ago. First, he was mistreated by a quack doctor with a crude operation, and then he was introduced to oral vaccines, claiming that they had the effect of "transmembrane sterilization." Mr. Wang had some medical knowledge and said that vaccines are external injection drugs, so how could someone take gonorrhea bacteria orally? He hesitated and could not decide, but the quack doctor still advised him to take them. Mr. Wang reluctantly took them, and instead of benefiting, he suffered. The urethra became blocked, and he felt distending pain and tearing. The perineum and anus were very sore. He was introduced by a colleague to me for treatment. After examination with a microscope, the mucous membranes of the affected area were covered with gonorrhea bacteria, like a mass of hair. Thus, inferior medicines that advertised "transmembrane sterilization" were proven to be a complete failure. I performed surgery and electrical therapy, and instructed him to take "Kelinong" to dispel gonorrhea, reduce inflammation, prevent putrefaction, and promote urination. After taking six or seven bottles, the disease finally subsided. After a blood serum test, there was no gonorrhea toxin reaction, thus proving that he was cured.

Former Professor of Nanyang Medical University

Doctor Zheng Yuanhe's Casual Talk on Lung Disease

Clinic: At the intersection of Ningbo Road and Sichuan Road

Clinic hours: 4 PM to 6 PM

To Eradicate Lung Tuberculosis Lesions, First, You Must Strengthen the Internal Defenses of the Lungs

Do you have lung disease?

When we talk about treating lung disease, everyone knows that we must kill the tuberculosis bacteria, and then other symptoms can be cured. This is naturally a fundamental solution. But how easy is it to kill tuberculosis bacteria? Because their outer skin is a layer of fatty substance, which is highly resistant to acid. No matter how good your medicine is in theory, it is difficult to penetrate this membrane and kill the bacteria.

Therefore, a German lung disease expert named Tu Mei, who was a specialist professor at a university medical school, always wanted to invent an effective lung disease drug. Based on the principle that tuberculosis bacteria are easily susceptible to medicine after their membrane is removed, he created a drug to remove the outer membrane of tuberculosis bacteria and mixed it with other antibacterial and tissue-regenerating drugs. Talking Points

Sudden Increase in Job Seekers in This City

— Jia Wei

A sudden increase in job seekers is another way of saying that there is a sudden increase in the unemployed. This is based on statistics obtained from the Employment Guidance Center, as reported by the *Ta Kung Pao* a few days ago. Since this month, the number of requests for consultations and applications for job registration at the Guidance Center has been increasing daily. The maximum number has reached eighty or ninety people per day, and the minimum has been more than fifty. On average, the total is around sixty people per day. It is said that the reason for this sudden increase is partly due to the unemployed seeking employment and partly due to school graduates. Because this month is the end of the term for various schools, students who have completed their studies are rushing to register, which has caused the numbers to increase sharply.

I remember that several months ago, newspapers published the number of unemployed people in this city in 1935, issued by the China Branch of the International Labour Office, which totaled more than 600,000 people. If we take the city's population as three million, then one in every five people is unemployed. However, this was only last year, and whether the estimated figures they obtained are accurate is still questionable. However, with the sudden increase of fifty or a hundred job seekers every day, we can see the general seriousness of the unemployment problem even more clearly.

Here, we believe that the sudden increase in job seekers today is largely due to the fact that various schools are in summer vacation, which has led to graduates who have completed their studies having to go to the "employment agency" to register first, because of the situation of "graduation is unemployment". Although they have finished talking and registering today, they still do not know on which day, which month, or which year half a seat will become available for them to squeeze into.

However, unemployment, unemployment, this phenomenon is by no means "always existed" - it should be known that in the primitive era of "drinking blood and eating fur, living in caves", human beings were living in a collective social life of "common labor, common distribution". Therefore, at that time, there was no such thing as "employment", and of course, there was no "loss" of it. However, today, with the rise and development of capitalism, this phenomenon - the unemployment problem - has become one of the serious social maladies that cannot be concealed in modern countries around the world. Moreover, before the economic system in capitalist countries, where the methods of production and property relations are always contradictory, is reformed and improved, this unemployment phenomenon will not go away for a single day.

However, in our country, which is known as "vast land, abundant resources, and numerous people", it cannot really be called a capitalist "civilized society". On the contrary, it is a completely semi-colonial social and economic organization. Therefore, for many years, under the various "cooperation", "assistance", and "support" provided by various capitalist powers competing for us in terms of economy, politics, culture... we have indeed benefited a lot from them. For example, the reason why this city has become one of the major commercial ports in the world and is honored as the "New York of the East" lies in this. However, the reason why the unemployment problem today is becoming increasingly serious also lies in this!

Isn't that so? Today, the so-called "New York of the East," Shanghai, is far less prosperous than it was four years ago before the "incident." We not only have hundreds of thousands, millions of unemployed people being driven to the brink of hunger and death, crushing and struggling, and students who have "completed their studies" facing the danger of "graduation is unemployment," but also people who are temporarily employed are worried about the arrival of the god of unemployment. Don't you see? The countryside is bankrupt, the cities are withering, and factories are closing down one after another, shops are liquidating, tightening, laying off employees... and even the expansion of puppet organizations and the rampant "special trade"... and so on!

Therefore, we believe that it is not only Shanghai, and it is not only "the end of the semester," that this serious number of unemployed people will continue to increase sharply, spread, and extend indefinitely, unless we urgently and thoroughly transform this semi-colonial economic organization...

A Visit to the China Relief Society for Women and Children’s Orphanage (Continued)

— Fang Zhou

The children are managed by the auxiliary birth group of the orphanage, with each person in charge of ten children. The auxiliary birth personnel are selected from the women living in the orphanage. There is also a hygiene group, which specializes in cleaning and is divided into three groups, A, B, and C, each responsible for four hours. However, there is also a reward for those who perform this work. However, the hygiene group in the outer courtyard is staffed by boys.

Further in is the sewing room, where several old women are mending torn clothes. The storage room is where various clothes and supplies are piled up. On the left is the bathroom of the outer courtyard. Next to a large hall is a small dining room, where people with infectious diseases and other illnesses eat.

As for the inner courtyard, it is next door, separated from the outer courtyard and the kindergarten. There is also a dining room, a bathroom, and dozens of bedrooms here. The situation is similar to that of the outer courtyard, but the equipment is slightly different. And some of the girls are working on sewing machines, while others are embroidering or doing other things.

After visiting all the places for a week, when I returned to rest under the grape trellis in front of the office, I raised a few more questions, such as: the procedures for entering and leaving the orphanage, the situation of girls choosing a partner, the way out for boys, and the skills and production learned by the students in the orphanage.

Mr. Pei's reply: The boys and girls in the kindergarten here were originally transferred from the Public Concession Police Station, so there are no procedures for entering the orphanage. However, if there is an unfinished case or other reasons that require a court hearing, the orphanage must send someone to accompany them. Those who enter the orphanage must also be questioned and investigated in detail by the orphanage. If they have relatives, they will be taken away. If they are in another city, the orphanage will send someone to return them. If they really have no one to rely on, they will be officially allowed to stay in the orphanage, but they must go through a month of training in the education class first. As for leaving the orphanage, anyone whose family comes to pick them up can leave at any time. However, those who want to leave the orphanage must have been there for more than a year and have a proper place to go before they can be allowed.

Girls choose their partners once a year, but it is entirely with their consent. The orphanage is only in the position of a guardian, and those who do not want to choose a partner are allowed to do so. When boys reach a certain age, the orphanage will find ways to introduce them to various occupations or recommend them to work in factories.

While in the orphanage, in addition to assigning some labor service, girls are taught skills such as sewing and embroidery, and boys also have manual exercises. However, the work they do is rewarded by the orphanage to encourage them.

Students in the orphanage are absolutely forbidden to leave their own courtyard step, and if anything happens, they must be accompanied by the auxiliary birth personnel to the office to negotiate. Only the auxiliary birth personnel and the hygiene group can move freely in the orphanage.

Now, seventeen or eight of the kindergarten students in the orphanage have eye diseases. I hope that the authorities of the orphanage will pay attention to this. (The End)

Watermelon Stall

— Sheli

July, a scorching day.

People are waving their fans and complaining about the sun. Lao Wu, the watermelon stall owner, is sweating all over, but he is happy in his heart: seeing such a big watermelon, it sells out in less than half an hour, and he is happy to grin and smile. He has to thank the hot weather and the sun.

Every summer, when watermelons are on the market, Lao Wu's stall appears on this street corner. He has been doing this business for several years, and he knows almost everyone here. The people who come to buy his watermelons are all his regular customers.

Yellow-fleshed, thin-skinned big watermelons,

Three copper coins for a piece.

Lao Wu shouts this every day. Many passersby are attracted by his shouting, so they run over, throw down three copper coins, buy a piece of watermelon, and eat it. Lao Wu shouts even more vigorously.

This year the weather is particularly hot, and the power of the sun seems to melt the world, and even the leaves of the sycamore trees by the roadside are drooping. Lao Wu wipes his sweat with a towel, thinking happily:

--Damn it, God willing, if I sell this season, I can pay off my old debts!

However, that morning, when Lao Wu picked up the watermelon load again, ready to set up his stall, he found something more on the sidewalk opposite. It was a white lacquer cabinet, with large red letters written on the front: "Tianjin Sour Plum Drink." A canopy was stretched over the cabinet with a wooden frame, and there were also two potted plants with green leaves. A tall man stood majestically behind the potted plants.

Lao Wu's heart suddenly became unhappy, even a little resentful of the tall man. He shouldn't have set up here, stealing his Lao Wu's business. But later, he saw that the tall man's business was not very good, and although his own stall was a little less busy than yesterday, there were still many customers, and his previous resentment and unhappiness disappeared.

--See if you have the ability to pull my customers over.

He simply looked down on the tall man.

But the next day, he suddenly realized that the number of customers in front of and behind the tall man was gradually increasing, while very few people came to his own stall. After inquiring, he immediately knew that the tall man had reduced the price of sour plum juice, selling it for only three copper coins a cup, and it was iced. Lao Wu was so angry that he just rolled his eyes. After thinking about it, he had no choice but to reduce the price as well. He wiped the sweat that was about to flow to the corner of his mouth and shouted anxiously:

Big and sweet watermelons,

Only two copper coins for a big piece!

This shout was like a void, and the people walking by ignored him and walked past in a hurry; some turned to the opposite side.

--This dog! He's simply trying to kill me!

If he doesn't avenge this, can he still be considered a man?

He stared at the tall man with his two eyes.

The tall man had no business at this time, and he was also staring at him.

--What are you looking at me for? You son of a bitch!

The tall man walked over.

--Who are you cursing?

--What if I curse you? Go bite my balls!

He also greeted him, his face flushed, and breathing a little heavily. The tall man didn't say a word, and with one hand he slapped him, causing him to take a step back. He still wanted to rush up, but, thump! The tall man punched him in the chest and knocked him down, and overturned the stall, and watermelons rolled all over the ground.

--Good! Good job! If you're a good man, wait for me, don't run away!

He struggled to get up, picked up the watermelons on the ground, and said this as he left.

--Wait for your mother, call her here.

The tall man sneered and went back to the opposite side.

The next day, Lao Wu didn't come to set up his stall again, probably because he was injured and lying in bed at home!

Chongqing's Sedan Chair Carriers (Part 1)

— Zijing

—Chongqing Correspondence—

"What a Chongqing city, the mountains are high and the roads are uneven, climbing uphill is exhausting, riding in a sedan chair is like riding the clouds."

This is a popular folk song in Chongqing. From this folk song, you can know the importance of sedan chairs in Chongqing's transportation.

Chongqing is a commercial port in the upper reaches of the Yangtze River, and it is also a strategically important mountain city in Sichuan Province. Looking up from the river bank, the layered city houses and streets are all placed on cliffs, which is very dangerous and unusually high. People who grew up in the foreign concessions of Shanghai, even if they don't feel the "difficulty of the Sichuan road," will be shocked that it is a geographical miracle.

Because it is a city built on mountains, the streets are all sloped, rugged, uneven, and it is really exhausting to walk! For people who grew up in the city, relying on their own footsteps to solve transportation problems is not only detrimental to the face of urban people, but also uneconomical in terms of time. However, geographical relations have determined Chongqing's fate. Not only can the latest streamlined cars not be transported from Kuimen for driving, but also the rickshaws pulled by manpower cannot run freely on the uneven streets. As a result, a large group of sedan chair carriers who ran from the countryside to the city to find food were born. In order to survive, they did not care about their sore muscles. They sold blood and sweat, carried people in sedan chairs to exchange for food, and solved this serious transportation problem for Chongqing.

The number of sedan chair carriers in Chongqing is just like the rickshaw pullers in Shanghai. These sedan chair carriers all come from the countryside. Most of them are hired farmers and tenant farmers in the countryside. The former works for the master (commonly known as long-term helper), and the average annual wage is only a hundred strings of cash. The higher wage earners, such as the so-called "senior long-term helper", are also only a hundred to two hundred strings of cash per year. Converted into Sichuan provincial currency, the annual income is only a few yuan to a mere ten yuan. If it is a single man, it can still be muddled through. If there is an unhappy wife at home, or if he is unfortunate enough to give birth to three sons and four daughters, then they rely on these few yuan to maintain the lives of several members of the whole family. If they don't starve to death, they have to sell a few of the scrawny children. Therefore, these hired farmers, under such tragic circumstances, cannot but try to find other ways to make a living. As a result, they went to the city in large groups. The latter is no different from the hired farmers. Most of them borrowed a hundred or ten strings of capital at high interest rates, rented a few pieces of dry land from the landlord, and planted some miscellaneous grains to maintain the lives of a few people in the family. If the year is good, the harvested grain, in addition to the landlord's rent, can barely cope. If they encounter a year of disaster, or the warlords start fighting, then they are finished! Their hopes pinned on those few pieces of dry land are completely shattered! Not only is there no hope of harvesting, but even planting is impossible! However, the landlord's rent is still to be paid. In their painful groans, they have no choice but to leave the countryside and slip into the city, each carrying a beautiful hope and joyful longing.

Because of the need, these sedan chair carriers occupied a very important position in Chongqing some time ago. They came from hundreds of farms, and they already had experience in carrying sliding poles. Moreover, some of them had strength. Therefore, after arriving in this mountain city, they all practiced an amazing skill of carrying sedan chairs. They have a copper-ribbed iron-boned waist, a pair of thick and strong arms, and a pair of flying legs that walk like the wind. The secret of carrying sedan chairs is the eight words "the waist should be hard, the legs should be soft." This means straightening the waist to maintain the stability of the sedan chair, and softening the legs to increase the speed of walking. When they walk on flat ground, the person sitting in the sedan chair feels as comfortable as sitting in a car slowly driving on an asphalt road. If it is uphill, that is a good opportunity for them to show their skills. The person in front tries to use both hands to drag the sedan chair from the shoulder to the back, and the person behind tries to raise both hands to support the sedan chair at the rear. In this way, even when climbing uphill, the sedan chair will maintain a considerable balance, and the person in the sedan chair only feels relaxed and ascending upwards, floating like riding the wind in the void. When going downhill, the former raises and the latter lifts, and the sedan chair just falls steadily downward, like being in a light balloon falling in the air. Only those who have experienced it can taste that kind of pleasure.

In the abyss, a cruel thought suddenly came to his mind, "Yes, kill myself! I have been working hard all day long, but I still can't get a full meal or a peaceful night's sleep!" His tears flowed down, and he glanced at his old mother and wife. In the corner of the wall, he saw his dazed children, looking at him with frightened eyes. Yes, their father was usually so majestic! But today he also cried as if they had suffered a little grievance in the past. They didn't know that their father was suffering a heartbreaking pain at this time.

But Li Cheng immediately had another thought come to his mind: "Yes! Suicide is the most undesirable act of a coward, no, it is the act of a shameless person. A young man will never be subdued by a bad environment, and he should have the responsibility to transform the environment. Yes, how could I have thought of such a shameless thought?" He wiped the tears flowing on his cheeks. He said to his old mother: (To be continued)

Little Chicken Little Lamb

(1) Little chicken, little chicken, where did you get the rice, where did you get the rice, to fill your belly, the rice from the Northeast is a treasure, rich in fat and nutrition, the output is the largest in the world, but, that place is already under the iron hooves of the enemies, little chicken, little chicken, you don't have to cry, you don't have to make a sound, there will always be a day when the situation is reversed, and the sun will shine again, so that you can eat as much as you want, and be happy.

(2) Little lamb, little lamb, where did you get the grass, where did you get the grass, to feed your hunger, the grass from Changbai Mountain, is fragrant everywhere, growing everywhere, shady green and dense like a green gauze tent, but, that place is no longer our homeland, little lamb, little lamb, you don't have to worry, you don't have to be sad, there will always be a day when we recover our homeland, and the old country is safe, so that you can eat as much as you want, and be happy forever.

Ballad Singing

Qian Jingzhang, Qian Zuixian, Mao Family Book

Zhongxi (1040), 10:00 AM to 10:45 AM

Opening: "Wenxuan Searches the Nunnery"

Wenxuan, a loyal and righteous young lad,

Searches for his master at the nunnery, sad.

He looks everywhere, no trace he can find,

Tears stream down his face, leaving him blind.

He stumbles upon the Guanyin Pavilion,

Kneels on the prayer mat, begging for salvation.

"My master's gone, no news to share,

The mistress at home is in despair.

She scolds and beats me without reason,

Saying I'm foolish, beyond all season.

She gave me a deadline, again and again,

But I don't know where my master has been.

Today's the deadline, it's drawing near,

If my master doesn't return, I fear,

I'll be sent to court, to face the rod,

My death is nothing, blessed by God,

But pity the mistress, so anxious and frail,

Great compassionate Guanyin, who never fails,

Show mercy, save us from this plight,

Grant my master a vision, day or night,

Advise him to return to his wife,

To avoid discord, and end the strife.

Let me escape unjust suffering's sting,

And my name, with my master's, will sing.

By imperial decree, the nunnery will be adorned,

Wenxuan cries his heart out, forlorn,

His deep sorrow touches the heart,

Silently pitying the young boy's part.

She wants to appear, to offer aid,

But fears the nuns will be betrayed.

The taste of marriage she has not known,

In two or three days, he'll turn home alone.

Perhaps the boy won't face death's doom.

He Yunfang, He Qinfang, Double Pearl Ball

Lin Ji (122), 2:15 PM to 3:00 PM

Opening: "Gold and Beauty"

What moves the heart with ease?

Gold and beauty, if you please.

Gold can sway the common man's will,

A beauty's words, like an imperial skill.

See how many youths have fallen low,

For gold and beauty, this much we know.

Remember Xiang Yu, the hero bold,

At Wujiang, his story's told.

Reluctant to part from his beloved Yu Meiren,

Look at corrupt officials, vying for power within,

They crave gold, never ceasing,

Some brothers fight, their bond decreasing,

Some murder for wealth, their souls defiled,

Some turn against loved ones, love exiled,

Some couples are separated, lands apart,

Some lose conscience, a blackened heart,

Some lose virtue, sacrificing all,

Gold, you hold such power, causing our fall,

You incite evil, with supreme might,

Harming so many, day and night.

You invert right and wrong, with great force,

So gold can buy a beauty, of course.

See how beauties of old held magic sway,

Overturning kingdoms, leading astray.

Remember Tang Jieyuan in "Three Smiles,"

He gave up love for beauty's wiles.

In "Double Pearl Phoenix," Wen Bizheng sold his soul,

To the Heavenly Official's door, losing all control.

He didn't want to be a scholar, you see,

But a low-ranking servant, for all to glee.

Don't laugh, Wu, don't look down,

Who doesn't love beauty, in every town?

Beauty, you're hateful, abusing your power,

Only valuing silk robes, in every hour.

For you, siblings turn against each other,

For you, fathers and sons cause a bother.

I think, if you weren't in this world,

Thieves wouldn't run wild, their banners unfurled.

If you weren't in this world,

We could strengthen our bodies, make our nation world.

If you weren't in this world,

No more inheritance disputes, no lives hurled.

If you weren't in this world,

Families wouldn't revolt, their stories unfurled.

All because of gold's dazzling gleam,

All because of beauty's alluring dream.

See how most men desire beauty's lure,

And women crave gold, forever pure.

So they deceive and love, for gold and silver's gain,

How many heroes die, in endless pain?

Countless are born, for your sake,

To dominate, to manipulate, to break.

Zhou Zhenyu, The Righteous Demon's Tale

Yuanchang (1120), 12:45 AM to 1:30 AM

Opening While Ill (Mimi Collection Inaugural Issue)

Confined by illness, years drift by,

Wasting my body, and my heart sighs.

I recall the days of spring illness,

When tender branches, lacked nature's kindness.

How long ago, the cicadas sang, outside the pearl blinds,

In the green gauze window, coolness finds.

Osmanthus fragrance mixed with medicine's scent,

The phoenix tree's fall, autumn's sentiment.

Now, fallen leaves and cold winds bite,

I know the earth slumbers in the winter's night.

Time wasted in illness, a blurred scene,

Spring departs, winter turns, a fleeting mean.

By the lonely lamp, a slender shadow's stretch,

Medicine stove and tea pot, a constant sketch.

Sleepless nights, I toss and turn,

Deep thoughts linger, lessons I learn.

Bitter, sour, spicy, sweet, all in one,

Separation, joy, sorrow, my fate outrun.

Bitter indeed, illness never ceases,

Hateful indeed, medicine always increases.

Sad indeed, the moon doesn't shine, who will care,

Tragic indeed, merciless rain's despair.

Few hours of sleep, but keen perception,

Sinking deep, tears shed with reflection.

Now I say, don't think my body is weak,

Look at the world, its woes speak.

A minor illness, will pass with spring,

Movie News

The Descendant of the Qing Dynasty, Princess Deling, Plays a Character in "The Good Earth"

— Lai

Pearl S. Buck's "The Good Earth" has long been known worldwide. MGM started filming it three years ago. They came to China to shoot funeral scenes and other Chinese folk customs. Later, because director George Hill committed suicide, it was shelved for a long time. Filming resumed a few months ago and is now in full swing. Now there is another eye-catching news item: the role of Lotus in the film is said to be played by Princess Deling. Although the contract has not been signed, it is a fact that the princess is auditioning. It is said that Princess Deling studied drama under the guidance of French actress Sarah Bernhardt, and also studied dance with American Ms. Duncan. This is news published in the Hollywood film magazine Cinema. The truth is yet to be confirmed, but if it becomes a reality, then this female role related to Chinese national dignity will be played by Deling.

Note: Sarah Bernhardt was a deceased famous French actress, whose reputation was probably even greater than that of Mei Lanfang in China. Ms. Sarah's performance in "La Dame aux Camélias" was once very popular. As for Ms. Duncan, she was a pioneer of classical dance in the United States and a proud student of Wagner, the founder of classical dance.

"Little Men," Unanimously Recommended by European and American Newspapers

Screening at the Cathay Theater starting tomorrow

"Little Men" is an immortal masterpiece by Ms. Alcott, praised alongside her "Little Women" and "Good Wives." It has now been adapted into a movie, starring an all-child cast from Hollywood, making it a rare treasure among American films in recent years. The film will be screened at the Cathay Theater starting tomorrow. Here are some excerpts of the excellent reviews of the film from famous European and American newspapers for the readers.

"Little Men will always touch your heart!"

"It is the most precious of American romance films!"

"Love, peace, moving, beautiful... Only Alcott's pen can richly render these."

"Popular with all... It can shock the world on the screen as well."

"It will make you smile knowingly... and make you yearn unconsciously."

"Undoubtedly one of the big films of the year."

"It is the most lovable and glorious of Alcott's works."

Second Factory

"Hearts United in Life and Death" and "Qingming Season" to be filmed simultaneously

The Star Second Factory on Avenue Albert has been established for nearly a month, and the interior decoration of the studio has been completed. "Hearts United in Life and Death" and "Qingming Season" (starring Liming Hui) will be filmed simultaneously. "Hearts United in Life and Death" is currently catching up with Chen Boer's scenes. The male lead, Yuan Muzhi, has recently been studying the makeup of the prisoner in the play. Based on Muzhi's past makeup experience, there will definitely be many amazing contributions in this play.

First Factory

"Night Meeting" and "Eternal Smile" being filmed simultaneously

At the Maple Bridge General Factory, "A Begonia Red" has been completely filmed, and "Xiao Lingzi" is being edited. "Night Meeting" (directed by Li Pingqian) written by Yao Sufeng and "Eternal Smile" (directed by Wu Cun) written by Liu Na'ou are being worked on in a tense atmosphere at the same time. "Night Meeting" stars Gu Lanjun, Gong Jianong, etc. Gong Jianong plays a blind man in this film. "Eternal Smile" stars Hu Die.

Odds and Ends

The "Spring Color" bi-weekly magazine published nine photos of Li Lili in a swimsuit in front and back, "sensual and beautiful", "only selling for eight cents".

It is said that in this year, "rumors" have become a bit "incomprehensible".

"A Begonia Red" writes a story that begins in the warlord era. There is a military governor from that era, and his "battle map" and photos of women he planned to "conquer" were actually compiled into a large album. At that time, the conversations among those military officers and bureaucrats mostly came from the ranks of women. "A Begonia Red" is a very interesting and very real exposure of a kind of corrupt and poisonous officialdom black screen.

Lan Ping starring in Cai Chusheng's new work "Wang Laowu", the conditions have been roughly agreed upon, and the contract can be signed within days.

The wolves needed in "Records of Cold Moon and Wolf Smoke" will be borrowed from zoos in various places.

The cast list for Yi Hua's new film "Guangling Tide" has been finalized. The leading actors are Yuan Meiyun, Wang Yin, Kai Xuan, Zhu Fei, etc.

The inaugural issue of Shanghai Beach Semi-Monthly Magazine was published today. The content mainly focuses on drama and film, and other topics such as dance, opera, broadcasting, and children are also covered. The editor of the magazine, Liu Yawei, extremely welcomes "objective and rigorous discussions".

Zhou Xuan performed at the Hongri Swimming Pool yesterday. Her diving posture was excellent and attracted much attention.
